id='poem_sentence_0_1216661'>勘会，准大元帅府参议都总管宝文牒：今后四方州郡凡有事宜，并申兵马大元帅康王行府与决施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216661_comment'></div>契勘管下湖州知州赵中大到任旬日身死，见任通判冯奉议为患中风，在假多日，本州知通并阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216661_comment'></div>缘湖州通彻太湖，接连宣、徽等州，昨来方腊作过，本州曾有陆行儿啸聚千馀人，致烦王师诛讨，人情惊疑不安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216661_comment'></div>兼严州遂安县见有贼人倪从庆聚众惊劫，相去不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216661_comment'></div>又四月初七日，承太平州等处关报到江宁府被群贼在府钉上城门放火，杀人作过，与湖州最为邻近，合行措置把截，以备冲突。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216661_comment'></div>今来起发勤王弓兵数多，全阙防托，若候差到正官知州，窃虑目今防托有失措置，必致误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216661_comment'></div>据本州士民经诸司陈状，欲差寄居朝议大夫新江东路提点刑狱莫砥逐急权摄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216661_comment'></div>诸司契勘本官委有材略，累经朝廷任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216661_comment'></div>检照昨承东道都总管司牒，备准尚书省劄子节文，令择人分总四道，各付以一面，吏得废置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216661_comment'></div>已具状申东道都总管司乞指挥外，今欲乞详酌特赐指挥，就差本官知湖州，或且令权摄，候有正官到日罢权，须至申闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216661_comment'></div>右，谨具申兵马大元帅大王行府，伏乞特赐指挥施行，伏候王旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216661_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1216661'>〔小贴子〕昨为事出几速，申东道总管司外，一面权令本官先次管领州事，伏乞照会。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1216661_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216662' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216662' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216662?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申大元帅府乞令监司同共承行军期状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216662")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216662_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216662'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216662'>勘会本路先为诸州自去年秋冬及今春，节次起发过防秋系将不系将兵、土军、弓手及勤王人兵，州县丞阙防托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216662_comment'></div>近于去年十二月内，严州遂安县广洲源倪从庆聚众作过，节次杀伤军兵及巡尉押队官不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216662_comment'></div>近又承镇江府太平州关报，四月一日江宁府凶贼窃发，见今据守江宁府城，事势大段凶恶危急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216662_comment'></div>本路正系邻路镇江府湖州接界，相去止是二百馀里，窃虑贼人别有奸谋，猖蹶侵犯，理须先为堤备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216662_comment'></div>兼不住承准太平州牒，欲要会合策应，虽事属安抚司，若止据见在弓兵官吏尽守常法，委是无可准拟，恐致误事，合逐急添差官及募兵，与逐处知通同共措置把隘出战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216662_comment'></div>安抚司不敢独自擅行，遂于四月十一日会合转运、提刑、提举常平、市舶、茶盐司就杭州权暂选差官属，将浙西一路军期合行事件从长相度，同共连冲行下所属州军施行，候事毕日依旧分司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216662_comment'></div>已具申奏外，缘都城壅隔，诏令未通，恐失几会，难以等待，仍逐急一面行遣，今来再合申禀行府者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216662_comment'></div>右，谨具申兵马大元帅大王行府，伏乞王旨特赐指挥施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1216662_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申大元帅府拘系两浙提刑季龙图状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216663")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216663'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216663'>四月二十四日，安抚司使臣姜安仁自京师回，称体问得张邦昌僭窃位号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216663_comment'></div>某契勘朝奉郎、直龙图阁、两浙路提点刑狱公事季质系是邦昌女婿，本官并妻等见在越州本司居住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216663_comment'></div>寻牒浙东安抚使，将季质并家属拘收赴所司严密防守，听候申取兵马大元帅大王指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216663_comment'></div>已承回报，将季质并一行家属尽拘送越州右狱收禁，止绝亲属出入，几察书信往来外，某又虑管下诸州府有似此亲戚，合行几察拘管，亦已牒杭、严、湖、秀、常州、平江、镇江府觉察施行，须至申闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216663_comment'></div>右，谨具申兵马大元帅大王行府，伏候王旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1216663_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216664' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216664' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216664?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申大元帅府乞总决万务状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216664")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216664_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216664'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216664'>右，某等今月二十四日，安抚司使臣姜安仁自京师回，伏闻金贼悖逆，都城失守，太上皇帝、皇帝陛下出狩朔方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216664_comment'></div>闻问震惊，陨涕颠越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216664_comment'></div>恭惟我宋太祖肇造区夏，列圣世世以德相承，岂意犬羊遂肆凶毒，渎乱天纪，遽至于斯，凡在率土含生之伦，孰不悲愤感泣，痛心疾首！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216664_comment'></div>伏惟大元帅大王，上皇之爱子，皇帝之介弟，躬受明哲，天资忠义，翼辅王室，功大德隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216664_comment'></div>昨自总戎，方布昭威命，式遏横溃，声动迩遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216664_comment'></div>今者大驾未还，号令壅绝，人心危疑，未知攸济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216664_comment'></div>伏望思国家艰难之业，副中外系望之情，镇抚四方，总决万务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216664_comment'></div>然后申饬尽瘁死节之士，奋励戡难勤王之师，图雪大雠，奉迎二圣，恢崇宝历，永康兆民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216664_comment'></div>某等被荷国恩，久尸荣禄，迫于忧愤，敢竭忱诚，谨具状，遣官奔诣行府申闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216664_comment'></div>某等不胜惶惧激切、虔祈恳祷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216664_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1216664_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216665' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216665' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216665?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申大元帅府乞移军浙右状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216665")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216665_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216665'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216665'>右，某等窃见金贼凶毒，陵犯王畿，兴复宗祊，当在旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216665_comment'></div>恭惟大元帅大王义当念祖宗基业之重，察华夏欣戴之心，总决四方，镇安民庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216665_comment'></div>然而汴都密迩贼境，频年轻犯，无所畏惮，今又累月蹂践之馀，人情危疑，民力耗弊，府库空竭，衣冠流亡，则再造之图，安可复处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216665_comment'></div>某所部浙西，外连江淮，内控闽岭，负山带险，左右湖海，东南本根，实为要会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216665_comment'></div>自唐末钱镠保全一方，既纳款归顺，民至于今，无大兵革，俗知忠义，人慕耕桑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216665_comment'></div>伏望行府观变察时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216665_comment'></div>从权虑远，趣下严令，暂戒东来，于苏、杭之间定择所驻，命忠勇大臣总领勤王之众留守京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216665_comment'></div>俟二圣回驾，中外乂安，徐图北还，以正王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216665_comment'></div>某等考之古今之宜，察之士民之论，万全永图，莫良于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216665_comment'></div>目睹利害，不敢隐默，谨遣官恭诣行府陈请，仰祈王慈，速决大计，阖境士民，延首听命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216665_comment'></div>干冒斧钺，不胜虔祈恳祷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216665_comment'></div>谨具状申闻，伏候王旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1216665_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216666' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216666?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申大元帅府缴纳告谕军民榜牒状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216666")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216666'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216666'>勘会金贼围逼京城，太上皇帝、皇帝出狩朔方，诏令壅绝，中外痛心，无所容措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216666_comment'></div>大元帅康王总戎于外，功大德隆，宗庙所依，群情共属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216666_comment'></div>当所已同诸司遣官躬诣行府，陈请总决万务，镇安人心，及移军浙右，经理中原，以俟大驾北还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216666_comment'></div>仰惟祖宗肇造区宇，几二百年，德泽在人，天命方永，岂容犬羊，终肆悖乱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216666_comment'></div>正仰天下贤智忠义之士枕戈待旦，力雪雠耻，迎还二圣，兴复大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216666_comment'></div>今肉食之列，皆世被国恩，爵秩廪食，其谁之赐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216666_comment'></div>生养安息，自何而得？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216666_comment'></div>兴言及此，孰不感愤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216666_comment'></div>凡我同志，各率其职，协力尽瘁，谨守封土，和辑兵民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216666_comment'></div>明示大义，毋使奸宄乱常，阴怀顾望，窃伺间隙，妄兴兵戎，以振扰善良，狃惑诈伪，以陷溺非僻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216666_comment'></div>一心戴宋，有死无二，以待王命之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216666_comment'></div>修城池，练士卒，聚粮饷，备器械，毋安苟简，毋玩阔疏，以戒不虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216666_comment'></div>宽赋歛，简役使，明犒赏，慎刑辟，毋纵侵扰，毋私喜怒，以吁众志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216666_comment'></div>庶几逆顺之理，各识所从，安危之图，咸思下逮，闾阎畎亩，亦获安生，以无忘我祖宗、上皇、皇帝之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216666_comment'></div>然后纠集义旅，与天下共讨凶逆，宏济艰难，俯尽臣子之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216666_comment'></div>须至移文牒请照会施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216666_comment'></div>谨牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216666_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1216666'>今告谕士庶兵民：金贼逆乱，太上皇帝、皇帝暂狩河北，诏令未通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216666_comment'></div>京师见迎请大元帅康王还京，当所亦同诸司遣官前诣行府，陈请总决庶务，北迎二圣，兼乞移军浙右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216666_comment'></div>今者国家虽遭金贼凶悖，大元帅康王见拥兵百万，袭逐追击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216666_comment'></div>尔等或在学校，或在闾里，或在田野，或在军伍，衣食居处，宗族子孙，生养安息，一民以上，无非被受国家二百年恩德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216666_comment'></div>睹此艰难，宜当悲愤感泣，痛彻骨髓，一心戴宋，死生不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216666_comment'></div>访闻河北百姓皆以白绢为旗，刺血上书「怨」字，迎杀金贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216666_comment'></div>都城里巷儿童各办小车，装载乾粮，迎接圣驾，已据探报，凯旋回京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216666_comment'></div>惟我东南之人，素识道理，天资善良，闻此必皆奋励，愿自效力，分别逆顺，与天下四方共修臣节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216666_comment'></div>中间恐有奸猾小人幸灾乐祸，鼓唱浮言，结集徒党，欲劫掠财物，报复私雠，惊扰城市，据守山林；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216666_comment'></div>或传导诈伪文字，阴怀顾望，诳惑上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216666_comment'></div>皆是昏迷，自取杀戮之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216666_comment'></div>尔等今日纵未能为国报雠，尽杀金贼，岂忍自同犬豕，弃绝君亲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216666_comment'></div>亦须更相几察，密切告官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216666_comment'></div>惟是人人感愤，不忘祖宗、太上皇帝、皇帝之德，乃可保家安身，永得名为忠义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216666_comment'></div>今沥血诚明以晓告，更望年德长上晓事父兄，开谕后生，教导愚民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216666_comment'></div>如有违犯，当以军法从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216666_comment'></div>右，各仰知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216666_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1216666'>右，某勘会自前月二十四日承报京城失守，太上皇帝巡狩朔方，宰臣张邦昌僭受伪命，盗据位号，臣子之义，不胜痛愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1216666_comment'></div>寻于二十七日遣官赍状躬诣行府，申乞总决庶务，移军浙右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1216666_comment'></div>去后又牒本路并邻境帅臣、监司、州县，令和辑兵民，各坚一心，无得顾望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1216666_comment'></div>又出榜戒告士庶兵民，推广祖宗德泽，示以逆顺大义，使不忘归戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1216666_comment'></div>相继体问得本路提刑季龙图出巡在本州，系是张邦昌亲女夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1216666_comment'></div>某即牒本官归越州本任，仍连牒浙东安抚使翟汝文拘收本官并家属送所司拘管，密切几察亲戚书信往来，听候王府指挥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1216666_comment'></div>又行下本路，更有张邦昌亲戚，亦依此施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1216666_comment'></div>又检会二圣车驾未还，张邦昌僭窃在位，四方事宜见并申取王府指挥与决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1216666_comment'></div>其京师传到递角诸般文字，自去年闰十一月二十五日以后至今，系是伪命，并不得传送承受，恐有透漏，过□牒逐州知州亦不得施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1216666_comment'></div>目今内外无不感念祖宗恩德，自某告戒文榜一出，虽诸营军卒与里巷妇人小儿，亦皆感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1216666_comment'></div>仰见国家蟠结人心，至深至厚，忠义之诚，人皆自守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1216666_comment'></div>惟日延颈，恭听王府号令，祝望两宫还阙，兵民并皆平安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1216666_comment'></div>所有牒、榜二道缴连在前，谨具状申大元帅府，伏乞照会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1216666_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1216666_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216667' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216667' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216667?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申大元帅府乞差江东西等六路帅臣状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216667")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216667_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216667'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216667'>右，某勘会自金贼犯顺以来，经今将及半年，所在州军起发过勤王弓兵之后，守御防托之人例皆阙少，全仗逐路帅臣措置弹压，各谨封守，共相维持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216667_comment'></div>今来体访得广东安抚使孙俟、湖南安抚使郭三益、福建路钤辖江常皆被召赴阙，缘道路未通，并在扬州等候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216667_comment'></div>江西洪州钤辖姚宗彦总领勤王人兵前去京畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216667_comment'></div>日近又据镇江府申，江东安抚使宇文粹中于四月初一日被军贼作过，未见下落，江宁府城见关闭据守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216667_comment'></div>湖北荆南府钤辖邓壅亦闻遭江贼破陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216667_comment'></div>东南形势，要害惟在江东、江西、湖南、湖北，外连福建、广东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216667_comment'></div>目今六路并无帅臣，窃虑见在盗贼无畏惮，及伏藏奸恶，互相观望，乘虚窃发，则东南数千里之地全无倚仗，远近人情日久艰危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216667_comment'></div>某忝在邻路，义不敢嘿，欲望特赐详酌，逐急于淮浙寄居官内选择有材识智谋、曾经擢用委寄之人，各令权领州事，听候朝廷别差正官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216667_comment'></div>或且令孙俟、郭三益、江常各归广州、潭州、福州本任，等候京师解围，依元降指挥赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216667_comment'></div>庶几逐路人心各有所恃，奸恶不敢萌心，且捕捉收复事有所任责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216667_comment'></div>事实机速，利害不细，不避狂愚之罪，敢辄陈述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216667_comment'></div>谨具申大元帅府，伏乞火急速赐施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1216667_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年5月</a>　在知杭州任，五月，又有奏状。作品：《倪从庆已降状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏乞分送倪从庆等三十四人近边州军自效状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏招捕倪从庆统领官等功赏状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏乞添置严州遂安县弓手状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏乞发杭州勤王人兵状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216537' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216537' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216537?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏倪从庆已降状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216537")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216537_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216537'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216537'>右，臣去年十二月十七日部内严州遂安县百姓倪从庆等，妄以勤王为名，聚众约一千五百馀人，占据本县广洲源作过，前后累次杀伤官吏军民不少，意欲仿效方腊侵扰州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216537_comment'></div>除已累具奏闻外，勘会本路弓兵两经起发勤王之后，所存拣残人数多不堪用，臣昨自到任，即行下所部州县团结保伍，专一几察盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216537_comment'></div>窃发之初，即令起邻近地分保甲，及招募土豪部领把截，又逐急差委本县寄居朝奉郎詹大和作统领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216537_comment'></div>因此群贼不能出洞，在外奸猾亦皆不敢趋附，声势无由增大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216537_comment'></div>缘贼居山岭深阻，道路狭隘，止通一人往来，不可深入，用兵非利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216537_comment'></div>兵力既少，又自正月半后，阴雨连并两月馀日，山路险滑，雾气昏塞，遂累于正月初七日、十七日出犯淳安县界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216537_comment'></div>二十九日，杀死经制司使臣何虤等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216537_comment'></div>至三月初九日，詹大和会合诸处弓兵分路进讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216537_comment'></div>又值当日阴雾，诸路兵到不齐，官军至洞口斗敌溃散，亦有杀死兰溪县尉王禹度等，贼愈更恃险凶恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216537_comment'></div>遂两具奏截留经制司福建枪仗手一千七百馀人相添使用，广设方略，别图约日讨荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216537_comment'></div>仍先出文榜招喻胁从之人，各令束身归投，与免罪复业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216537_comment'></div>至三月十三日，因白马保甲余再兴等杀退一阵，始稍知惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216537_comment'></div>又统领官密遣人诱说贼用事腹心姜光祖、胡国度二人拘留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216537_comment'></div>四月初七日，会合弓手、枪仗手六千馀人并入，其贼徒遂止据险拒抗官军，不敢迎敌，因此穷蹙，于初八日具状乞降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216537_comment'></div>臣以农蚕是时，守把之人久废作业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216537_comment'></div>见承江东关报，江宁府群贼据府城为变，本路镇江府、常、湖三州并是邻接，相去皆二百馀里，分兵防托不及，难以专事从庆，已一面从其请，许令悔过，率众勤王，依资格借官补授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216537_comment'></div>今据统领官詹大和等申，贼首倪从庆并从党甲头姜光祖等五十二人，并已出洞公参，官兵见皆退寨，一方已得平定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216537_comment'></div>谨录奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216537_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1216537_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216538' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216538' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216538?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞分送倪从庆等三十四人近边州军自效状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216538")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216538_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216538'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216538'>右，臣勘会严州遂安县凶贼倪从庆等三十四人虽已降，差官管押前赴行在，原其本意，实因朝廷多事，所在起发过勤王弓兵，守备单寡，凭恃源洞深险，乘虚窃发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216538_comment'></div>鸣鼓一呼，一源之内八百馀户、一千二百馀人无不响应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216538_comment'></div>从庆为之魁首，何通、叶善、方忠、徐周为之左右，姜光祖、胡国度、胡国史等皆尝为进士，为之谋主，其馀号为大甲头、小甲头者二十馀人，并在今出降数内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216538_comment'></div>偶因臣预先团结保伍，得以几察，分布守把，内外控制，其谋不行，遂止坚守巢穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216538_comment'></div>续见官兵会集，四面围守，势力穷蹙，方肯归降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216538_comment'></div>然前后累次杀伤官员人兵不少，其人皆凶恶狡诈，各有武艺，雀鼠之智，足以□□一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216538_comment'></div>勤王之请，假以为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216538_comment'></div>今既示大信，特从宽贷，若依旧得在本土，未能保其终不生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216538_comment'></div>窃虑到行在，见金贼已退，放散诸处勤王人，随例发回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216538_comment'></div>欲望圣慈详酌，特降睿旨，将此三十四人假以近下名目，并令分送近边州军，使之自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216538_comment'></div>若果能知过尽力，随其所长，亦有可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216538_comment'></div>若长恶不悛，尚怀他心，便各因事诛之，朝廷威信况自不失两全，东南一方可以永绝后患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216538_comment'></div>狂愚冒犯，上浼天聪，臣不胜惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216538_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1216538_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216539' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216539?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏招捕倪从庆统领官等功赏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216539")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216539_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216539'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216539'>右，臣勘会严州遂安县凶贼倪从庆已招降，除累经战阵有功并把隘防托合行推赏人等见取会类聚保明申奏外，所有臣先于寄居见任官内委请统领、计议、措置、监捕，始末一行官五员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216539_comment'></div>内一员统领官朝奉郎詹大和，前因方腊作过时，说谕本县广洲源百姓余熙、白马源百姓徐连，使不从贼，保全一方，曾经朝廷转官推赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216539_comment'></div>方本县杀死县尉，擒捕知县，贼势始炽，人莫敢当，大和承臣公文，更不辞避，即时团结保甲，分布四面，内御贼众，外察奸党，遂至贼不敢冲突出外，亦无胁从附丽之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216539_comment'></div>二月初九日，弓兵失利，本县奸民唱率，将起应贼，大和亲斩首五十馀级，方获安帖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216539_comment'></div>相继召募武勇保甲，会集弓兵，入图攻讨，别遣土人入洞招诱贼党腹心用事人，终能致贼悔过乞降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216539_comment'></div>一员，本司干办公事、承奉郎王嘏，系方腊时保护秀州、没于王事大将王子武之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216539_comment'></div>自二月初承本司差管押邵武军枪仗手，将臣措画方略与詹大和同共计议，尽心遵行，不顾危难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216539_comment'></div>其二月初十日，遂安县民户惊扰逃避，嘏连夜徒步走淳安县，分取枪仗手前来救护，人情赖以弹压，获免变乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216539_comment'></div>续同詹大和分布大兵进讨，及招诱投降，躬亲护押降贼前来本司，并无疏虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216539_comment'></div>一员，宣教郎、前河北河东路宣抚使司干办公事、权转运司干办公事梁泽民，儒林郎、管押邵武军枪仗手江佃，统领邵武军枪仗手在淳安县界港口，正系出入之路，分布营寨，教习兵民，独当一面三月馀日，防托守御，贼众不敢侵犯县界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216539_comment'></div>一员，宣义郎、权遂安县林师说，统领泉、建州枪仗手，据罟纲溪，正当贼巢穴之冲，亲领兵众，宿食寨内一月馀日，贼众因此退避，两县藉以为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216539_comment'></div>三人亦同预计议招贼就降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216539_comment'></div>前件功力次第，实不可诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216539_comment'></div>臣窃见昨方腊作过，当朝廷无事，一路兵力全备之时，将佐尽在，所部不乏使令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216539_comment'></div>然凭陵州县，如蹈无人之境，官兵莫可抵捍，例遭杀戮，遂致远近响应，陷没六州二十七县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216539_comment'></div>蒙朝廷遣童贯、谭稹将带西北骁将刘延庆、王禀、杨惟忠、何瓘、辛兴宗等亲总劲兵十万馀人，或降或诛，方获平定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216539_comment'></div>今来倪从庆等作过，乃在金贼犯顺、内外震扰之际，州郡三次起发勤王弓兵，所在空虚，将佐随兵前去，使臣材武人又先已尽起赴阙，人情惊疑，奸宄观望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216539_comment'></div>詹大和等元非当职任事之人，偶因臣逐急委请，乃能同心国事，尽瘁竭力，纠集乌合之众，初无制节之令，固守把截，使不得冲突猖蹶，残害生灵，讫至纳款归降，保全两路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216539_comment'></div>较之方腊，事势轻重难易，数倍不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216539_comment'></div>臣误当帅阃，人微望轻，不能预为镇抚，以致盗发部内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216539_comment'></div>若非藉此五人，无以逃责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216539_comment'></div>欲望圣慈详酌，特降睿旨，令与等第推恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216539_comment'></div>虽见危致命，臣子之常情；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216539_comment'></div>然有功见知，大君之美意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216539_comment'></div>因以风示四方，使伏节死难之士皆识圣心恢远，虽远必闻，虽细必录，则人人奋励，各思自效，在于今日，不为小补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216539_comment'></div>狂愚冒犯，上渎天听，臣无任惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216539_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1216539_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216540' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216540' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216540?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞添置严州遂安县弓手状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216540")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216540_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216540'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216540'>右，臣近承遂安县统领官朝奉郎詹大和状，备坐到提刑司牒，倪从庆等聚集作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216540_comment'></div>缘遂安县地分阔远，多系高山峻岭，穷谷深源，控扼去处管额弓手止计六十人，显是数少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216540_comment'></div>窃虑讨荡倪贼之后，要得弓级分头巡警盗贼，镇压民心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216540_comment'></div>今相度欲添置弓手六十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216540_comment'></div>臣勘会逐县弓手役法虽有定额，今来军兴之际，盗贼窃发，所在不同，理合随宜增损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216540_comment'></div>其遂安县弓手若更添六十人，通旧一百二十人为额，巡察一方，消弭奸恶，实为经久利便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216540_comment'></div>除已行下严州权暂依准提刑司牒，先次召募逐急应副使唤，及关牒提举常平司施行外，伏望圣慈详酌，特降睿旨施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216540_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1216540_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216541' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216541' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216541?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏起发杭州勤王人兵状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216541")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216541_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216541'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216541'>右，臣勘会，近准发运司牒，闰十一月十三日蜡弹，枢密院劄子备到圣旨：金人围逼京城，诸路州军皆令统率军兵及民间强壮等人速来应援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216541_comment'></div>闻命忧愤，寝食皆废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216541_comment'></div>寻行下所属州府，将见管厢、禁军拣选材勇有事艺、堪披带出战之人团结，并依准指挥，便宜以人数立武官，借加官格，召募善部辖人，择民间强壮人散行纠集，根刷军器及应干州县诸司钱斛，桩办粮食盘缠，各欲择日躬亲管押赴京城听候使唤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216541_comment'></div>次近据严州申：有遂安县百姓倪从庆、徐周等妄以勤王为名，占据本县广洲源，杀死县尉，擒捉知县前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216541_comment'></div>日近大段猖蹶，已有众数千人，侵突淳安县界，焚烧屋宇，杀伤保甲，虏掠居民，妄戴黄伞，见谋直来冲犯杭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216541_comment'></div>兼昨准去年宣抚司关报，探到金贼欲取山东前来两浙作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216541_comment'></div>若帅臣、监司尽赴阙庭，窃虑奸恶乘间窥伺，惊扰州郡，浙西一路，不保安危，重贻朝廷之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216541_comment'></div>今来逐急措置，先将杭州及诸司团结到厢、禁军并纠集到民兵，共二千人，刬刷到盘缠犒设□，及别桩办三月钱粮，共四万七千贯文，变转轻赍物、军器一千八百事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216541_comment'></div>选差到武节大夫、荣州刺史、兼閤门宣赞舍人、秀州钤辖邓珍充统领官，于今月二十一日起离前赴京城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216541_comment'></div>如是道路尚有未通，即令随所在计会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216541_comment'></div>宣抚使范讷、东道副总管朱胜非、经制使翁彦国交割所有辖下其馀州府，见今不住催促，节次起发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216541_comment'></div>臣等不获身先士卒，效命矢石，瞻望阙庭，不胜惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216541_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1216541_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年6月</a>　在知杭州任，六月，续有奏状。作品：《奏乞添置徽严衢三州巡状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏乞差人至高丽探报金贼事宜状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏江宁府营造乞从简约状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏乞措置濒海州县防秋状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏乞鄂州建帅府及修江宁府等五城状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏乞弓手免他役及教阅激赏状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏乞禁罢献纳借贷指挥状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏措置招募弓手狀》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216543' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216543' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216543?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞添置徽严衢三州巡检状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216543")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216543_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216543'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216543'>右，臣近准遂安县统领官朝奉郎詹大和状：昨因方腊为乱，有深山顽恶人从贼作过，朝廷宽恩，诛戮不尽，至今尚有怀奸小人潜相连结，乘隙啸聚，极为不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216543_comment'></div>其严州遂安县至徽州休宁县二百里，又至衢州开化县一百六十里，三州市井相去隔阔，山路险远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216543_comment'></div>其地名有昏源、松阳源、方吴源、赤口、龙山等，皆是素来小人屯聚结集之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216543_comment'></div>今来倪从庆作过，其松阳源余仲轲等已聚众欲窃发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216543_comment'></div>虽已斩获，窃虑久远不便，欲于三州界首龙翔寺前添置巡检一员，招募土兵一百五十人，以备控扼防托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216543_comment'></div>又据严州通判、监捕官、朝议大夫吴煇状：倪从庆等结集徒党固已有素，州县未易得知，诚以贼居巢穴，山岭深邃，遽难几察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216543_comment'></div>今广洲与白马源相接，重山复岭，道径窄狭，贼众据守，弓兵未易敢入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216543_comment'></div>相度贼平之后，欲于广洲、白马源人烟居止处添置巡检一员，招募土兵一百二十人，所贵可以弹压一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216543_comment'></div>臣寻行下严州勘会诣实，及专委本司干办公事、承奉郎王嘏躬亲体究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216543_comment'></div>今据王嘏申，上件两处委是山川险隘，人迹不通，自来凶恶小人凭恃啸聚，合依逐官申请，保明是实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216543_comment'></div>臣检会自来严州以东盗贼，皆是依凭地利，敢肆凶恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216543_comment'></div>昨方腊就擒，后来帮源洞已蒙朝廷添置巡检一员，至今别无他变，实赖其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216543_comment'></div>若因事稍增巡捕之官，自无所容，实为经久利便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216543_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降睿旨施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216543_comment'></div>其三州界就龙翔寺前创置廨宇，以徽严衢三州巡检为名，广洲、白马源就赵侯庙后创置廨宇，以本地分乡名凤林巡检为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216543_comment'></div>所有招募土兵，并依逐官元申请为额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216543_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1216543_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216544' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216544' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216544?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞差人至高丽探报金贼事宜状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216544")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216544_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216544'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216544'>右，臣窃惟善用兵者莫先于广耳目以明斥堠，善觇国者莫深于审形势以察情实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216544_comment'></div>盖耳目广，则意之所不及，有愈于意之所及；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216544_comment'></div>形势审，则迹之所不见，有出于迹之所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216544_comment'></div>此不可不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216544_comment'></div>春秋之时，秦欲伐郑，师次于滑，郑商人弦高遇之，密以告郑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216544_comment'></div>穆公得闻而警，因以囿田之事谢秦客，孟明知其有备而不敢进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216544_comment'></div>郑之使秦者不知其何人，而逆为之备，以捍其锋，遂以保国，乃得于逆旅之商人，非意之所不及有愈于意之所及者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216544_comment'></div>汉高帝欲击匈奴，使者十辈皆以为可，惟奉春君知其匿壮士健马，以为欲见短，伏奇兵以争利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216544_comment'></div>高帝不之信，乃以三十万众困于平城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216544_comment'></div>以高帝之智，而不能详奉春君之言，以汉在廷谋臣策士，而惟奉春君能测匈奴之隐，非迹之所不见有出于迹之所见者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216544_comment'></div>窃见金贼阴怀不道，欲为封豕长蛇，荐食上国之日久矣，燕晋疆吏初不以时闻，至前年冬，金师大入，将欲渡河，而京师始知之，其罪固不容诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216544_comment'></div>去岁解围之后，朝廷宜少警矣，然八九月之间，尚闻持和议以为必成，而谓秋冬决不复再入，傍观者为之寒心，而庙堂以为得计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216544_comment'></div>此虽玩习苟简，更相观望之过，然亦耳目不广，形势不审，有以致之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216544_comment'></div>此天下所共痛愤而不能释者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216544_comment'></div>臣所部浙西并浙东路，并外连海道，与高丽跨海相望，去贼境不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216544_comment'></div>顷闻贼有妄窥东南之意，若北自登莱，东假高丽，扬帆而来，或出于两浙，皆远不过二十日，近五七日可至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216544_comment'></div>臣自到任，常有私忧于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216544_comment'></div>本州舶船旧许与高丽为市，间有得与其国人贸易者，往往能道其山川形势、道里远近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216544_comment'></div>因令舶主张绶招致大商柳悦、黄师舜问之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216544_comment'></div>二人皆泉州人，世从本州给凭贾贩高丽，岁一再至，留高丽者率尝经岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216544_comment'></div>因为臣图海道，大略言：贼境旧与契丹苏州，正直登莱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216544_comment'></div>高丽东北与贼接界，有关门为限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216544_comment'></div>贼旧事高丽，每岁入关，即遣使进奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216544_comment'></div>崇宁三年，始与高丽称兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216544_comment'></div>大观元年，高丽遂取其六洞于南境，以筑九城，实以甲兵粮食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216544_comment'></div>后复为贼以沉罗黑水堆洞人夺之，自是与高丽绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216544_comment'></div>政和五年，契丹为贼所败，取其沿海六十馀州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216544_comment'></div>高丽乘间诱得贼用事首领一人，贼屡来求，不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216544_comment'></div>及贼灭契丹，宣和七年，高丽复遣使通好，为贼留不归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216544_comment'></div>去年，贼扰我畿甸之后，高丽遂两遣人使贼，贼亦两报之，并欲使之称臣而修贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216544_comment'></div>正副使共二人，其一为契丹人，其一为金国人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216544_comment'></div>高丽去年亦自为其外大父谋篡，焚其宫室、积聚、器械甚广，不能如前日之盛，见出避于别都，势恐不能与贼重抗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216544_comment'></div>然贼所得契丹傍海六十馀州，皆荒陋单弊，其地与高丽隔鸭绿江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216544_comment'></div>每岁冬深，鸭绿江冻，冰厚可胜车马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216544_comment'></div>此皆柳悦等亲供说如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1216544_comment'></div>臣既有闻，不敢隐默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1216544_comment'></div>窃以郑弦高之事观之，柳悦等虽商贾冗贱，然在高丽久，所听探皆得其国人之言，初本无意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1216544_comment'></div>若因使伺贼，万一欲谋扰我，或得其道里所出、期会所定，或其国中自有变乱，先事而达，有出于我耳目所不及、形势所不见者，则不为小补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1216544_comment'></div>辄肆管见，欲委此二人，许以名目，阴令如常岁之高丽贾贩，应得贼中动息，皆亟使来告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1216544_comment'></div>俟参验得实，有补于事，即厚赏旌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1216544_comment'></div>责以军令，无得张皇漏泄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1216544_comment'></div>其人皆感奋愿自效，欲以此月末渡海，约冬初复还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1216544_comment'></div>臣以申奏不及，已一面各权借以承信郎名目，给与公据，令趁时前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1216544_comment'></div>伏望圣慈详酌，如有可采，乞降睿旨，密付臣施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1216544_comment'></div>边臣探报，深入敌境，虽理之常，然今跨海越国，创始之初，迫于几会，不先陈请，专辄自决，罪当万死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1216544_comment'></div>更乞矜察，以臣职守，粗欲图报，激于忠愤，别无他肠，特赐容贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1216544_comment'></div>所有柳悦等画到海外图一本，缴连在前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1216544_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1216544_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1216544'>〔贴黄〕臣伏闻朝廷见欲遣迪功郎刘蠡等使高丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1216544_comment'></div>臣虽不知遣蠡等所谋，然今来柳悦等止是因其贾贩，使密自刺贼动息，以广耳目，俟有实验，然后赏之，有利而无损，禁令无得漏泄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1216544_comment'></div>恐万一或得以为用，即于今来使命并无相妨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1216544_comment'></div>伏乞睿察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1216544_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216545' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216545' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216545?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏江宁府营造乞从简约状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216545")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216545_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216545'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216545'>右，臣备员从官，出守藩辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216545_comment'></div>近者尝以疾病，乞就闲秩，伏蒙圣恩，未即矜许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216545_comment'></div>既勉强承命，方时艰难，身睹陛下宵旰以图中兴之日，曾未有纤毫报效，夙夕愧惧，无以自处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216545_comment'></div>惟有随事纳忠，少图裨益，庶犹愈于缄嘿坐食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216545_comment'></div>故苟在职一日，不敢遽忘此心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216545_comment'></div>伏见经营建康以备巡幸，舍二百年定都之业，而即偏霸暂处之地，此诚不得已之下策，非出陛下本意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216545_comment'></div>然而天子以四海为家，古之帝王一岁而四巡狩，不以为难，则今万一顺动，固未为过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216545_comment'></div>惟无伤财，无动众，事不求备，居不求安，则何所往而不可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216545_comment'></div>窃闻今建康规画，有司似不能尽体圣意，道涂之言皆云，欲创建宫室，备列百司，规效京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216545_comment'></div>臣愚窃以为未然，此行幸，非迁都也，何遽如是哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216545_comment'></div>夫功大则费广，费广则民劳，此理之自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216545_comment'></div>几月以来，争传江东之民有家业钱一千而取三千者，田一亩而出方砖一片者，一邑而率砖灰土木之费以二十万计者，置窑烧砖而望青斫木者，甚有至于取平江府朱勔家之巧石以备玩设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216545_comment'></div>此虽未必皆实，然方陛下恢复之初，爱民恤下之意，如抚赤子，恶衣菲食之念，自比匹夫，此声岂宜闻于外乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216545_comment'></div>是殆州县之吏迫于期会，各课职守，规以自免过咎，而不暇为朝廷之思也，然所以为累者大矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216545_comment'></div>昔周以公叔带之乱，挟戎狄以伐京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216545_comment'></div>襄王出居于郑，使人告难于鲁，自称曰「不谷」，左丘明以为易服降名，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216545_comment'></div>非特王者为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216545_comment'></div>狄人侵卫，齐小白复之，文公衣大布之衣、大帛之冠，以临其国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216545_comment'></div>独务材训农，通商惠工，谨教劝学，授方任能，而卫复兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216545_comment'></div>故史称其元年革车三十乘，季年乃三百乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216545_comment'></div>下至于越王勾践，蛮夷之事，无足言矣，然及图报吴也，在国亲巡孤寡，而共其乏困，在军熟食者分而后敢食，所共尝者，卒乘与焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216545_comment'></div>居不重席，室不崇坛，器不彫镂，舟车不饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216545_comment'></div>故其未战也，父兄相与请曰：「越四封之内，亲吾君也，犹父母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216545_comment'></div>子而思报父母之仇，臣而思报君之雠，其敢不尽其力乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216545_comment'></div>及其将战也，则又父勉其子，兄勉其弟，妇勉其夫，曰：「孰是君也，而无死乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216545_comment'></div>于是败吴于囿，又败之于没，又郊败之，遂以灭吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216545_comment'></div>恭惟陛下以神圣文武之资，受天明命，奄有祖宗之大业，天下孰敢不服？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216545_comment'></div>即位以来，膏泽屡下，宽大之令日闻于人耳，哀痛之诏日感于人心，天下孰敢不归？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216545_comment'></div>蠢尔叛天不道之虏，合中国之力而共诛之，其殄灭必有日矣，何足惧哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216545_comment'></div>在陛下行之如何耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216545_comment'></div>乃者天申节上寿作乐，抑而不行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216545_comment'></div>贡奉之物非天地宗庙陵寝所须，却而尽罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216545_comment'></div>天下皆知陛下约己思艰之意，尧舜无以过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216545_comment'></div>然执事之吏乃复因缘旧习，过举如此，甚不称陛下盛德美意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216545_comment'></div>愚俗难以家至户晓，愿下明诏，显示戒饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1216545_comment'></div>应建康等处营缮，除城池楼橹以备守御，营寨次舍以待屯戍，粮糗储蓄以充禀给，金钱币帛以供犒赏外，其馀一切，乞从简约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1216545_comment'></div>无以险陋为不中，无以草创为非体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1216545_comment'></div>古者君在草莽，其臣皆反首茇舍，则百司庶府亦非求安之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1216545_comment'></div>陛下既屏声色而不御，抑侍卫而弗充，则外朝之制、后宫之仪，亦不必备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1216545_comment'></div>使天下晓然皆知陛下大雠未雪，不忘尝胆之心，二圣未还，常切承颜之念，则四海之内，苟非木石，食陛下之禄，沐陛下之恩，谁不欲毕命自效，弯弓而北向乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1216545_comment'></div>设有背德避患者，天下必共起击之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1216545_comment'></div>追迎銮舆，再造王室，复还千里之畿，归严九庙之奉，可尅日而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1216545_comment'></div>臣位卑人微，未尝得觐清光，遽冒君威，犯分不韪，罪当万死，不胜惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1216545_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1216545_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216546' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216546' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216546?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞措置濒海州县防秋状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216546")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216546_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216546'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216546'>右，臣备员一道兵民之寄，当朝廷艰难之时，外难未平，所仰四方相与维持者，其责尤重，不敢偷安尸素，苟且目前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216546_comment'></div>故自到官以来，日夜尽瘁，庶几少有寸补，不至上误使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216546_comment'></div>窃见金贼虽已遁去，封豕长蛇、荐食上国之意恐未遽弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216546_comment'></div>登、莱两州密迩其境，而两浙诸州例与海道相连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216546_comment'></div>自登莱航海，远不过数日可至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216546_comment'></div>浙西诸县如杭州盐官，秀州华亭、海盐，常州江阴，平江府昆山、常熟，浙东诸县如越州馀姚、上虞，明州象山、定海、奉化、昌国，温州乐清，台州宁海、黄岩，皆切近于海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216546_comment'></div>臣去岁守南京，尝得宣抚司探报，闻贼欲取山东路入两浙作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216546_comment'></div>是时彼方有意再犯王畿，势固未暇及此，然又见其未尝无此谋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216546_comment'></div>近有东道总领司尝被驱虏使臣归为臣言，贼知其为两浙人，颇问山川道里形势甚详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216546_comment'></div>又其所诱留人，多有东南篙工水手从事舟楫之间者，皆为陈说计策，及夸大苏杭富实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216546_comment'></div>臣益知犬羊贪婪之心，不无所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216546_comment'></div>今两河蹂践之馀，内至近甸，金帛子女掠取殆尽，使其溪壑之欲诚未厌足，则去岁宣抚司探报岂得不虑哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216546_comment'></div>两浙风俗轻而易动，有自来矣，又连遭方腊、倪从庆之变，人怀危疑，常不安居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216546_comment'></div>加以险僻顽民阴间伺隙，溃散冗卒居多啸聚，乐祸喜乱，未易制御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216546_comment'></div>今环两浙之地，濒于海者十几四五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216546_comment'></div>议者谓虏以铁骑冲突为长，泽国水乡非其便利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216546_comment'></div>此以其竭国来寇论之可也，若志但在金帛子女，则姑以千百之众，胁吾驱虏之人以为乡导，声言欲杂出于数州之间，以图侵掠，则未至，而吾民先已惊遁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216546_comment'></div>况乐祸喜乱之徒望风乘势，或应之以合谋，或假之以自奋，则其忧有不可胜言者，何必直须贼之尽至乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216546_comment'></div>晋之孙恩窃入上虞，唐之袁晁发自临海，近日方腊，山谷一夫，亦能破六州二十七县，皆已事之验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216546_comment'></div>然所以为备御之策，不过城池、器用、兵卒、粮食四事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216546_comment'></div>今防秋仅有两月，事势已迫，每事必俟朝廷措画，则势不及待，所以分忧捍患，尽其力而为之，惟在守令，而未见其可当此任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216546_comment'></div>臣虽误当帅事，法有常守，又浙东非所部，不敢辄有侵越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216546_comment'></div>若遂拱默不言，缓急或有误事，虽即诛死，何足偿责？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216546_comment'></div>辄敢冒昧陈列，欲望圣慈详酌，特降睿旨，先次遴择濒海诸郡守臣，各得其人，分命监司遍行巡察，及诸属邑，凡令长有不可委仗者，许得权宜移易罢黜，别加选辟，量立赏典，以为激劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216546_comment'></div>应所合指画事，除城郭已有近降指挥外，其馀如修治器械、训练弓兵，皆严为近限，责以实效，无令文具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216546_comment'></div>僻远之地，巡尉与弓兵或可增添元额，许一面差补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216546_comment'></div>将来如有调发，须量以分数存留，无阙守备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216546_comment'></div>钱谷移用，亦当桩管应用，无至侵夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216546_comment'></div>至于分布防托之宜，阖散战守之节，斥堠几察之要，邻比应援之期，皆须熟议素讲，预有一定之谋，相为表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216546_comment'></div>平居持重镇抚，不至于劳民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216546_comment'></div>有警随事酬酢，皆可以御敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216546_comment'></div>军声士气稍达于海外，使彼望而知畏，而吾境内之奸，亦有以逆折其心而不敢萌，则远近人心恃以不恐，朝廷亦可一意西北，而忘东顾之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216546_comment'></div>干冒圣聪，不胜惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216546_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1216546_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216547' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216547' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216547?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞鄂州建帅府及修江宁府等五城状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216547")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216547_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216547'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216547'>右，臣伏闻朝廷已命翁彦国经理建康，以备巡幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216547_comment'></div>窃惟国家定鼎汴阳，固万世无穷之计，然而圣虑深远，以为万一之备，或有不得已者，则形势所在，不可不考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216547_comment'></div>建康居东南要津，实恃大江以为险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216547_comment'></div>然自豫章而东、长沙而北、江陵而西，江行数千里，控扼之会，皆以武昌为襟带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216547_comment'></div>孙权建鼎足三方之势，抗魏制蜀，倚为用武之地，故周瑜、吕蒙因之以破曹操、擒关羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216547_comment'></div>晋元帝南迁，首命陶侃以龙骧将军为太守，故苏峻之乱，卒赖其效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216547_comment'></div>宋、齐之后，专事陇蜀，不以为意，侯景长驱，无所忌惮，遂致梁祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216547_comment'></div>唐以鄂岳为一道观察，尝委以重人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216547_comment'></div>至牛僧孺罢相，文宗复以鄂州为武昌军，置节度使，特命僧孺守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216547_comment'></div>则历代兼制江湖之意，形势大略可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216547_comment'></div>唐虽都关中，与吴晋异，亦不敢忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216547_comment'></div>至于所以夹辅建康者，又环之有五城，曰石头城，曰冶城，曰台城，曰苑城，曰新城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216547_comment'></div>盖大江之险，特可为之限隔，而所以守江者，必有为之捍御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216547_comment'></div>今惟新城在扬州之境，利害所系差轻，其馀四城皆不可废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216547_comment'></div>韩滉镇浙西，当朱泚之乱，潜修石头城，人疑其异志，亦可知石头城之为利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216547_comment'></div>臣愚窃谓鄂州宜建为帅藩，宿以重兵，以为建康之西门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216547_comment'></div>石头城当寻其故址，兴辑之，分备屯戍，以谨大江之守，然后建康可恃以固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216547_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特命大臣参议施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216547_comment'></div>臣职忝论思，虽事非所部，顾在今日，匹夫皆愿自竭，以冀秋毫之补，不敢以犯分为嫌，辄献其愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216547_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216547_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1216547_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞弓手免他役及教阅激赏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216548")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216548'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216548'>右，臣勘会乡村巡捉盗贼，专以弓手为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216548_comment'></div>元丰法，每十人，轮二人在县主当尉司公事，不得过七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216548_comment'></div>万户以上，十人月一替，仍不妨教阅、捕盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216548_comment'></div>二千户以下县，差二人充狱子，每二千户增一人，至五人止，半年一替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216548_comment'></div>遇有禁囚，与免教阅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216548_comment'></div>凡在官者，皆有白直，而县尉独不破白直，止称当直，盖防拘占之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216548_comment'></div>而当直人差出州界主管私事者，绍圣法有杖一百之禁，以理揆之，当公事固无不妨教阅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216548_comment'></div>既充狱子，固未尝无禁囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216548_comment'></div>是三分之一已废其职矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216548_comment'></div>而比年以来，岁久法玩，互相沿袭，其弊尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216548_comment'></div>本县巧作名目，差使或倍过本法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216548_comment'></div>而县尉私为借事，及以会问盗贼为名，役使于数百里之外者，公然无所畏惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216548_comment'></div>以故教阅既废，巡捕亦阙，小盗肆行，积为大盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216548_comment'></div>昨宣和三年，尝因臣寮建明立法：今后如违法差占，以违制论，不以赦降去官原免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216548_comment'></div>诸路固未必皆尝举行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216548_comment'></div>去岁复因专用元丰法，人益纵弛，冲改不行，防秋调发之后，但得免在县主当公事，其他未有禁约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216548_comment'></div>臣愚窃谓弓手既<span class='inlineComment2'>（缺四字）</span>盗，则在县主当公事与充狱子□宜废罢，非捕盗不得<span class='inlineComment2'>（缺六字）</span>准宣和法，科以违制之罪□请借事者<span class='inlineComment2'>（缺八字）</span>者许经所属州并监司陈告受<span class='inlineComment2'>（缺十二字）</span>以正兵□为一等，既日教阅，必责<span class='inlineComment2'>（缺十二字）</span>每十人□□钱一贯为银揲子，以<span class='inlineComment2'>（缺十三字）</span>谁肯劝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216548_comment'></div>亦当略相依仿，每岁并春秋两教委自安抚司<span class='inlineComment2'>（缺七字）</span>类聚按试，量以分数，取事艺高彊人给赏如正兵役省□钱充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216548_comment'></div>庶几人知激励，缓急可以倚仗，不至误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216548_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降睿旨施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216548_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1216548_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216549?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞禁罢献纳借贷指挥状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216549")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216549'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216549'>右，臣窃惟方今国雠未雪，连年用兵，外有方张未灭之虏，内有乘间窃发之盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216549_comment'></div>然而都城失守几月，陛下谦逊，未即大位，奸伪僭乱之人窃居大宝，天下内外远近卒无一人敢怀向背者，祖宗德泽二百年，蟠结在人，至深至固之效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216549_comment'></div>臣始闻二圣北狩，首移檄部内士庶兵民，喻以逆顺，推本国家根本灵长不拔之意，使各坚守一心，以待陛下之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216549_comment'></div>是时，上下方汹汹，臣言一出，虽武夫悍卒、妇人小儿，无不感泣愤励，所在聚观数百人，更相传告，以死自誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216549_comment'></div>臣以是占之，知吾宋之有天下，非特天命方永，在人心者固不可得而易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216549_comment'></div>陛下既嗣有大统，赦令继下，其爱恤元元，涵养抚存者无不备至，可谓知所本矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216549_comment'></div>应上供之数，非祖宗旧制而过取于民者，一切尽罢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216549_comment'></div>凡欠负之所当输者，不以贯伯名色，皆使蠲除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216549_comment'></div>民知散利薄征，陛下之诚意，弛负已责，陛下之仁心，其欢呼归戴，岂有已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216549_comment'></div>然臣尝观，自昔良法，行之无不在人，使其人守之，必先有以戒其渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216549_comment'></div>古之言曰：「作法于凉，其弊犹贪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216549_comment'></div>作法于贪，弊将若之何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216549_comment'></div>去岁渊圣皇帝继承之初，深监前日政事科扰之弊，而力去之，其见诏令者亦无所不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216549_comment'></div>然在位之臣不明大体，未几，以国用窘匮，乃开献纳金帛之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216549_comment'></div>其后金贼既迫城下，仓猝召勤王兵，虑调发不足，又使得以借贷于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216549_comment'></div>天下固知二令非出于渊圣皇帝，然郡县被受，能推广上德者无几，往往皆挟中旨，肆为诛求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216549_comment'></div>愚民悭靳，安知公上之急，谓之献纳者，未有不科敷而得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216549_comment'></div>此例一启，凡急而取于民者，无不以献纳为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216549_comment'></div>于是去冬及春，有或课以等第，或率以贯头，有一邑而出三五万缗者，有一郡而出二十万缗者，至于再、至于三不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216549_comment'></div>问之，则曰：「法固有之，此出于军须权宜，而民所乐输也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216549_comment'></div>岂其实哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216549_comment'></div>借贷之令，初虑官钱不足，而勤王之兵不可缓，故不得已命之，以备万一，然且使偿其岁租之半，亦固未有遽取之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216549_comment'></div>而所在不问府藏之有无，不论调度之多寡，畏监司者恐其劾问，为己谋者虑其后乏，迫期会而取办，废经画而仰成，则惟民之求而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216549_comment'></div>入有常数，用无常限，人得为市，高下在手，有上户释而下户及者，有此色薄而彼色厚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216549_comment'></div>簿籍不足考，券契不足凭，所蠲之租、所偿之期，尚安得而计哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216549_comment'></div>臣耳闻目睹，未尝不为朝廷惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216549_comment'></div>以谓科率之禁虽严，而掊刻者犹未戢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216549_comment'></div>搔扰之戒虽数，而困革者犹未苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216549_comment'></div>此虽有司之过，然不几作法于贪者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216549_comment'></div>昔汉武帝事匈奴，卜式愿输家财半佐边，公孙宏以为非人情，不轨之民，请勿许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216549_comment'></div>式后复以钱二十万给河南太守徙民，武帝召以为中郎，布告天下，尊显以风百姓，然卒不闻复有献者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216549_comment'></div>古今人情，大抵不相远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216549_comment'></div>唐德宗讨朱滔、王武俊，用韦都宾、陈京请，借商钱，期得五百万，可以支半岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216549_comment'></div>乃使赵赞行之，约罢兵而偿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216549_comment'></div>搜督既峻，民有自经而死，遮宰相诉哭者，长安为之罢市，然才得八十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1216549_comment'></div>其后泾原兵乱，大呼于市，果假此以藉口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1216549_comment'></div>既不足济所乏，徒以失民，得不偿失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1216549_comment'></div>今陛下以圣德启中兴，武帝、德宗之事固万无有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1216549_comment'></div>然二令未除，慢吏庸人终得以并缘为奸，以济其私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1216549_comment'></div>百姓何知，但见前日之习尚在，必将疑陛下之诏，以为虚文，而奸猾乱民之徒，或得因以扇惑其党，则所害为不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1216549_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特命有司明示诏旨，以前二令出于有司一时之请，自今无得复用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1216549_comment'></div>凡州县敛于民而称情愿、托军期而辄借贷者，皆重坐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1216549_comment'></div>使远近之民感恩怀德，皆能深信而不疑，则捍患扶倾，必有见危而思奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1216549_comment'></div>孟子谓三代之得其天下也，得其心，斯得民矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1216549_comment'></div>此正今日之先务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1216549_comment'></div>狂愚冒犯，臣不胜皇惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1216549_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1216549_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216550' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216550?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏措置招募弓手状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216550")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216550_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216550'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216550'>臣六月二十九日准枢密院六月十七日劄子节文：奉圣旨，江、淮、两浙路依河北、河东、京东西、京畿招置弓手，以备使唤，凡一切体格，路依河北、河东等路已降指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216550_comment'></div>并蒙连到河北等路添差县尉、使臣并弓手人额体格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216550_comment'></div>除已即时行下所辖州县，将边近河海及控扼附近合置差去处相度措置，别具奏闻外，今具画一下项，须至奏闻者：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1216550'>一、河北路即以河海为重，本路既不边黄河，其大江地分与海相通处形势均一，并须置差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216550_comment'></div>并控扼附近，可以侵突冲要之处准此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216550_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1216550'>一、创置之初，恐难□相应募数足，或恐不无抑配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216550_comment'></div>欲令逐县各择等第土豪，以人数分募，量为蠲其身役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216550_comment'></div>募及二百人，与免差保正副一次；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216550_comment'></div>一百人，与免差大小保长一次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216550_comment'></div>如有武艺，愿就充都头、十将者听，与其免终身之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216550_comment'></div>弓手能召募及五十人，长行与补押官，押官以上各逐升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216550_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1216550'>一、所用支钱粮数目浩大，若依旧法只用常平司钱，窃虑不足，理须与诸司钱那融使用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216550_comment'></div>候将来措置定，专令转运、常平两司应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216550_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1216550'>一、教阅并合依正兵七日法，县尉日躬亲监教，春秋两教如之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216550_comment'></div>遇有捕捉，牒本县令佐权监大教，安抚司委通判一员同准备□□诸县按阅，给赏亦合依正兵条例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216550_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1216550'>一、教习人数既多，合用军器□逐县量所管人数，于知县厅置甲仗库，各令以系省钱置造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216550_comment'></div>监□牒甲赴州作院制造外，馀枪刀之属，令知县厅躬亲监勒□□制造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216550_comment'></div>遇有使用，逐旋关取知县专掌出纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216550_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1216550'>一、指使一员，欲先选有武艺获贼有功人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216550_comment'></div>如无，次选实有武艺□勇人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216550_comment'></div>候将来弓手有都教头，年满换官人相兼差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216550_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1216550'>一、弓手既以防托江海，即须令兼习水战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216550_comment'></div>逐县各量置战船，每十日一次，知县、县尉同共教阅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216550_comment'></div>不得以按视为名，辄为游观燕集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216550_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1216550'>一、县尉廨宇旧多在州县城下，今既系两员，合令创置官于本界内往扼要害之地，量与巡尉远近得中处建立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216550_comment'></div>其营房支系省钱造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216550_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1216550'>一、县尉除捕盗检验外，本县应检估物产、定夺争讼之类，并不许差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216550_comment'></div>本州非缘军事，亦不许差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216550_comment'></div>应旧法不依常制许差法并罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216550_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1216550'>一、弓手有犯并逃亡等，并依军法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216550_comment'></div>因差出外而饮酒赌博斗殴，并加本法一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216550_comment'></div>县尉遇捕盗下乡，除日给饮食外，辄有须索卖买于乡村之人，并坐赃论，许人告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216550_comment'></div>故纵弓级等搔扰居民、乞觅钱物，而失觉察者，减犯人一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216550_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1216550'>右，谨件如前，伏望睿慈特赐详察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216550_comment'></div>如有可采，速赐施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216550_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1216550_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年7月6日</a>　在知杭州任，七月六日，复龙图阁直学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　在知杭州任，考两浙路山水源流，欲补《水经注》之阙失，会兵乱，不及成书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年8月1日</a>　八月初一，杭州兵变，石林被囚执。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年12月</a>　在杭州，当于十二月兵变平定后被释放。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4c378fc68f8249539796b92c720d21ab_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4c378fc68f8249539796b92c720d21ab");'><span id='4c378fc68f8249539796b92c720d21ab_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，53岁</div><div id='4c378fc68f8249539796b92c720d21ab' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月11日</a>　二月十日，至杭州，迎迓高宗于临平镇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月12日</a>　二月十二日，高宗至杭州，以州治为行宫。石林请罢升旸宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月14日</a>　二月十四日，在杭州行宫奏事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月18日</a>　二月十八日，在杭州行宫奏事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月20日</a>　二月二十日，在杭州，迁尚书左丞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月22日</a>　二月二十二日，在杭州，奏时当兵间，扈从车驾，礼宜简便。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月22日</a>　二月二十，在杭州，有奏札。作品：《奏乞募探事人赴左右司投状札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216560?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞募探事人赴左右司投状劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年2月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216560")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216560_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216560'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216560'>臣昨任户部尚书，伏奉御营使司劄子，奉圣旨，委臣措置召募知乡道、前去江北探报事宜人，押赴御营使司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216560_comment'></div>臣今来见赴都堂治事，恐措置选择不精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216560_comment'></div>契勘御营使司事并已厘正，其探事人合隶枢密院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216560_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后凡有应募人，并赴左右司郎官投状审验，择可委人逐旋押赴枢密院，准备节次发遣前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216560_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1216560_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月23日</a>　二月二十三日，在杭州，奏罢掊敛民财之军期司。作品：《奏乞罢州县军期司及剖刻民财等事札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216559' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216559' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216559?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞罢州县军期司及掊刻民财等事劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年2月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216559")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216559_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216559'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216559'>臣伏睹陛下渡江以来，引咎罪己，过形贬损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216559_comment'></div>将至杭州，首罢升旸宫，既又出宫人于□□三百八十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216559_comment'></div>内饔日膳一羊，每食殆无兼味；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216559_comment'></div>乘舆服御，十减八九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216559_comment'></div>戒惧勤俭之诚，可谓至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216559_comment'></div>臣昨待罪户部，虽府库之积仓猝焚劫殆尽，然驻跸东南，敢不上体圣意，养兵犒军之外，每事悉从省约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216559_comment'></div>经营收簇系官钱帛，旬日之间，稍已有备，未尝一金敢取于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216559_comment'></div>窃虑州郡之吏，或险肤之民，妄意测度，为见朝廷急阙，因仍已行之令，唱为浮言，规摇民听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216559_comment'></div>或谓有所劝诱，或谓有所科率，或谓欲借贷税租，或谓欲均敷官告，如此之类，远近不能无惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216559_comment'></div>伏望圣慈下臣此章，风示上下，使知陛下视民如伤之意，秋毫无所取给于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216559_comment'></div>今沿江守御，与近郡险阻控扼去处，皆已遣官措置，□馀近里郡县但修举常职，谨守封疆，可以无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216559_comment'></div>窃闻监司、州县或擅立军期司为名，讽喻迫胁，掊刻民财，亦乞尽令止罢，违者委御史台觉察纠之，重寘典宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216559_comment'></div>庶几民获安堵，感激奋励，皆怀卫上捍敌之志，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216559_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1216559_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月26日</a>　二月二十六日，在杭州，奏对，赠陈东、欧阳澈官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年3月3日</a>　三月三日，在杭州，因与朱胜非议事不合，罢执政。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年3月3日</a>　三月三日，在杭州，诏专一提领户部财赋，充巡幸顿递使，石林力辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年3月5日</a>　在杭州，约于三月五日，改命知洪州，石林复固辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年3月</a>　在杭州，三月，石林固辞不就命，遂奉祠退居湖州卞山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年3月</a>　三月，离杭州前，上奏札。作品：《奏乞抚定诸军无失机札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216561?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞抚定诸军无失机会劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216561")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216561'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216561'>臣伏闻诸军搜捉内侍，□扰城市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216561_comment'></div>幸而未至大段猖蹶，及今须速遣近臣早传圣旨，宣布德意，收集抚定，使各解退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216561_comment'></div>若更迁延时刻，窃恐无所归着，人怀疑阻，别生奸谋，比至日晚，则难措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216561_comment'></div>更乞遍召宰执入侍左右，从长观变，密定计议，无失机会，以贻后悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216561_comment'></div>臣罢居里巷，不获躬卫殿陛，瞻望天颜，不胜驰诚激切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216561_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216561_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1216561'>〔贴黄〕闻见今诸军各般取内侍家财物，亦乞就降圣旨，便令给与，以安其心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1216561_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
宜兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='222b574cb58e4b0e98956695ad090042_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("222b574cb58e4b0e98956695ad090042");'><span id='222b574cb58e4b0e98956695ad090042_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，53岁</div><div id='222b574cb58e4b0e98956695ad090042' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月</a>　二月，至常州后，旋经宜兴。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='711aeac06e5548fca41d7758edbb714f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("711aeac06e5548fca41d7758edbb714f");'><span id='711aeac06e5548fca41d7758edbb714f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>，56岁</div><div id='711aeac06e5548fca41d7758edbb714f' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>四、五月间，归卞山，过宜兴，游张公洞。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>四、五月间，归卞山，过宜兴，游善权洞。<br /></div>
