ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　在建康府任，年底，边报稍稀，夜坐西斋，有诗感怀。作品：《连日边报稍稀西斋默坐至夜分》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526637?labeling=true' target='_blank'>连日边报稍稀西斋默坐<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本下有至夜分三字）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526637")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526637'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526637'>鼓角遥闻出塞声，边风吹雁过高城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526637'>疆陲无复戊己尉，盗贼犹怜壬午兵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526637'>岁晚胡床闭深阁，夜长刁斗听连营。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526637'>便须从此传烽息，要及春农论劝耕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526637'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526637_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　是年，在建康府任，有奏状。作品：《乞晋卞将庙额状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216511' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216511?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞晋卞将军庙额状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216511")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216511_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216511'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216511'>右，臣伏见本府有晋尚书令卞壸墓一所，在城西南隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216511_comment'></div>谨按《晋书》，壸当南渡之初，与王导、庾亮实相成帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216511_comment'></div>苏峻之难，以壸都督大桁东诸军事捍贼，力疾再战，遂死于敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216511_comment'></div>二子眕、盱见壸没，相随俱死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216511_comment'></div>忠孝之节，萃于一门，成帝特赠壸侍中、骠骑将军、开府仪同三司，后复给钱修其茔兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216511_comment'></div>历代封植，载在祀典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216511_comment'></div>自金人渡江，残毁殆尽，窃虑岁久，渐致湮没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216511_comment'></div>臣已委官检计，重建庙宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216511_comment'></div>方时多艰，如壸等辈，数百年间不过三五人，宜有褒显，以诒后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216511_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特依应天府张巡、许远、蔡州颜真卿例，赐以庙额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216511_comment'></div>庶以兴起四方仗节死难之士，共明君亲之义。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1216511_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　是年，在建康府任，建忠烈庙，撰碑文。作品：《忠烈庙碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216777' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216777' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216777?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忠烈庙碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216777")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216777_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216777'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216777'>晋尚书令、赠侍中、骠骑将军、开府仪同三司卞公讳壸，字望之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216777_comment'></div>苏峻之难，父子皆死敌，墓在建康牙城之西、旧冶城之南、司命宫之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216777_comment'></div>历代奉祀惟谨，而庙貌不立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216777_comment'></div>伪唐保大中，始作忠孝亭于墓北，岁久夷圮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216777_comment'></div>庆历三年，龙图阁直学士叶公清臣复封植，立石为表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216777_comment'></div>后五十年，当元祐八年，天章阁待制曾公肇易亭为祠，图公像其中，载之祀典，春秋命有司从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216777_comment'></div>又二十七年，当绍兴元年，金人渡江之后，资政殿学士叶某蒙恩分镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216777_comment'></div>兵火初平，城郭丘墟，欲修二公之旧而未暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216777_comment'></div>又七年，大驾临幸还钱塘，诏即建康为留都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216777_comment'></div>上不以其老且无能，复付之宫钥，乃克即墓南度地为庙，请于朝，下太常，赐公庙额曰「忠烈」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216777_comment'></div>于是为正室三间，以设公像，列公世子赠散骑常侍眕、次子赠奉车都尉盱从公俱死者于傍，以侍中嵇公绍配食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216777_comment'></div>环以列庑，缭以周垣，增饰兆域名木，禁刍牧无得犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216777_comment'></div>工三月告成，躬率僚吏，奉少牢之奠，告于祠下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216777_comment'></div>初，建康之民去公远，莫能尽知公之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216777_comment'></div>及天子褒显暴耀，新宫屹然，衣冠咸会，于是士女奔走，欷歔太息，或至流泪，皆有感激奋励，知以身殉国之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216777_comment'></div>某曰：呜呼，礼义之感人，岂但教告驱率而后听哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216777_comment'></div>然世知公死之为难，而未知使公得生，必可以兴晋，而不克成焉，尤可惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216777_comment'></div>自古为天下，未有不合群力众智而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216777_comment'></div>其间必有卓然特立，超出一世之上，而不与之俱者，然后能矫拂一世之俗，以为之宗，而天下从之，则以治易乱，以存易亡，惟其所欲为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216777_comment'></div>东晋立国江左，孰不曰王导之功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216777_comment'></div>尝谓晋不能复中原、一天下，正导之罪，此其故何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216777_comment'></div>凡晋之失，在于祖虚诞而贱名检，乐侥倖而轻节义，眩华靡而略功实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216777_comment'></div>是以因循苟简，取给目前，讫至于乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216777_comment'></div>而导曾不能反是，乃欲因是以求济，其区区自救不暇，非导孰为之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216777_comment'></div>天下，大物也，物与物何足以相远？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216777_comment'></div>在《易》之《大过》曰：「泽灭木，大过，君子以独立不惧，遁世无闷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216777_comment'></div>孔子序《易》，至《大过》《既济》之际，为之说曰：「有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1216777", 1216777, "Clauses/105/Comments/2")'>过物</span>者必济」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216777_comment'></div>夫必有过之，乃能济之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216777_comment'></div>晋有三人焉：以身捍患，料敌制胜，曰温太真峤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216777_comment'></div>精诚远虑，明见事机，曰蔡道明谟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216777_comment'></div>维持纪纲，纳之轨物，则公而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216777_comment'></div>太元以后，天下事皆得道明谋之，太真行之，而公守之，虽内有王敦、苏峻，外有刘聪、石勒，其何能为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216777_comment'></div>不幸太真早死，而公仅效于一战，道明虽在，已不胜其众矣，此所以终其世不竞也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216777_comment'></div>因追考其事，论次为公庙碑，而系之诗，以遗后之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216777_comment'></div>公惟不亡，尚足慰其千载之意云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1216777_comment'></div>其辞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1216777'>五马渡江晋南奔，乾坤震荡四海昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1216777_comment'></div>孰扶此都创本根，茂弘陋矣安足论！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1216777_comment'></div>我评三士参高骞，为世作室身墉垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1216777_comment'></div>惜哉其类不得繁，神州陆沈无与援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1216777_comment'></div>弃捐名教资清言，颓波一律来浑浑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1216777_comment'></div>卞公特立尤雄尊，卒殉以身丧厥元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1216777_comment'></div>二雏从公如凊温，宁公已死身独存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1216777_comment'></div>公归在天朝帝阍，血面诉帝忠不冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1216777_comment'></div>岁时来临从旗幡，览观江山望中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1216777_comment'></div>从先二雏属櫜鞬，下睨豺虎犹齧吞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1216777_comment'></div>新宫崇崇俯前轩，揭名日星自今恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1216777_comment'></div>潢污之水荐藻蘩，哀歌节缓芬桂樽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1216777_comment'></div>祥飙飒然下修门，尚慰千载忠孝魂。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_1216777'></div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1216777_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　是年，建紬书阁，有纪文。作品：《紬书阁纪》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216762' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216762' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216762?labeling=true' target='_blank'>䌷书阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216762")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216762_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216762'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216762'>孔子曰：「仕而优则学，学而优则仕」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216762_comment'></div>古之君子，未尝一日不学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216762_comment'></div>故傅说告高宗，亦曰「念终始典于学」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216762_comment'></div>而譬学于殖，不殖将落者，原伯鲁之所忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216762_comment'></div>建康，承平时号文物都会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216762_comment'></div>绍兴初，余为守，当大兵之后，屯戍连营，城郭郁为榛莽，无复儒衣冠盖，尝求《周易》，无从得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216762_comment'></div>于是凛然惧俎豆之将坠，勉营理学校，延集诸生，得军赋馀缗六百万以授学官，使刊六经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216762_comment'></div>后七年，余复领留钥市廛，五方杂居，生聚之盛，虽非前日比，然询汉唐诸史，尚未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216762_comment'></div>顾余老且荒废，亦安所事简策？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216762_comment'></div>念汉初，去孔子世尚未远，一更秦乱，而《书》亡五十一篇，《诗》亡六篇，《周礼·冬官》尽亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216762_comment'></div>经且如是，而况其他？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216762_comment'></div>屋壁之藏，幸得保有其馀，至于今尚存者，学士大夫相与扶持传习之效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216762_comment'></div>今四方取向所亡散书，稍稍镂板渐多，好事者宜当分广其藏，以备万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216762_comment'></div>公厨适有羡钱二百万，不敢他费，乃用遍售经史诸书，凡得若干卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216762_comment'></div>厅事西北隅有隙地三丈有奇，作别室，上为重屋，以远卑湿，为之藏，而著其籍于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216762_comment'></div>退食之暇，素习未忘，或时以展诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216762_comment'></div>因取太史公金匮石室之意，名之曰「䌷书阁」，而列其所藏之目于左方，后有同志，日月增益之，愈久当愈多，亦足风示吾僚，使知仕不可不勉于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216762_comment'></div>干戈将息，而文治兴，有民人社稷者亦皆思读书，无重得罪于吾先君子之言云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1216762_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年1月</a>　在建康，正月初，有《与晁激仲夜话》等诗四首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《次韵答晁激仲》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《再答》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《又答》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526630?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与晁激仲夜话</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526630")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526630'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526630'>外家文采到诸郎，凛凛词锋未可当。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526630'>伴我何辞共戎马，怜君聊欲濯糟浆<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：激仲以池州酒正从余辟。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526630'>残年落寞风尘际，永夜从容银烛光。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526630'>祇恐扁舟吾欲去，病慵无意薄淮阳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526630'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526630_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵答激仲</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526631")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526631'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526631'>牛渚谁逢临汝郎，参军暂肯佐戎行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526631'>世缘不拟营三窟，人事那求馈五浆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526631'>春近岭梅横暗<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作素）</span>蕊，夜寒霜月落飞光。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526631'>十年情话何由尽，我亦<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作邑邑）</span>伤心叹渭阳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526631'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526631_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526632' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526632' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526632?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再答</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526632")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526632_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526632'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526632'>生涯久许捕鱼郎，凫雁相追不乱行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526632'>但遣陶庐有松径，不辞楚酒醉椒浆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526632'>交情老柏寒方见，妙语灵珠夜有光。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526632'>回首渐知归路好，已看梅柳动初阳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526632'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526632_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526633' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526633' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526633?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又答</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526633")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526633'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526633'>家声合继紫微郎<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，不独诗同沈鲍行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526633'>晚岁清谈淹幕府，中原喜气望壶浆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526633'>颇闻时论怜衰朽，空愧君恩负宠光。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526633'>肯许辋川期后约，弹冠知不借王阳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526633'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526633'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_526633_0'>⑴ 自注：晁氏自文元、文庄皆尝历知制诰，至以道，复为中书舍人。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526633_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年1月14日</a>　在建康，正月十四日夜，张旸叔、晁公昂相过共话，有诗感怀。作品：《山间每岁正月望夜梅花正开多与客饮花下今年郡廨独坐十四夜张旸叔晁激仲相过共话宣和间事慨然归不能寐因以写怀》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526642?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山间每岁正月望夜梅花正<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>开多与客饮花下今年郡廨独坐十四夜张旸叔晁激仲相过共话宣和间事慨然归不能寐因以写怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年1月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526642")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526642_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_526642_0'>① 四库本作后梅花盛</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526642'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526642'>山头野梅白玉花，月明弄影纷横斜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526642'>青天无云万峰立，下有十亩幽人家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526642'>年年春归不暇省，但扫雪径寻寒葩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526642'>老夫已忘少年事，灯火岂念更繁华。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526642'>一杯起步遍空谷，破屋归卧暾朝霞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526642'>陪都复来亦何有，凛凛杀气浮高牙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526642'>重关深锁夜漏永，忽记昨梦翻长嗟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526642'>景龙门前一月会，金碗赐酒馀雄誇。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526642'>神州陆沉近归我，汉节方议通胡沙。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526642'>天翻地覆那得料，忍复更听渔阳挝。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526642'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_526642_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年1月</a>　在建康，正月，以肺气屡发，上章请退闲乞宫观。作品：《第一次乞宫观第一状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>第一次乞宫观第一状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216512")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216512_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216512'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216512'>右，臣昨者误被圣恩，起之闲废，付以留钥，实具恳辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216512_comment'></div>两蒙御前金字牌降到指挥不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216512_comment'></div>怵迫就职，今已半年，仰赖朝廷威灵，边隅无警，内外军民，偶获安静，出于天幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216512_comment'></div>伏念臣少苦多病，众所共知，久屏山林，心志彫落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216512_comment'></div>昨被命之初，已曾一二缕陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216512_comment'></div>去岁兼以夏秋服凉药过多，入冬肺气喘满，寒嗽屡作，至今未平，尤难勉强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216512_comment'></div>若犹贪冒久居，必致旷败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216512_comment'></div>今来已及解严，伏望圣慈特赐哀怜，许臣依旧宫观，退即散地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216512_comment'></div>不惟陪都要藩，免误重寄，亦于臣投老，进退之义，陈力不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216512_comment'></div>庶几保全晚节，不致重犯清议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1216512_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年1月</a>　在建康，正月十七日前后，有书与梁汝嘉。作品：《与梁仲模论榷货物书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年1月</a>　在建康，正月，有启回霍蠡。作品：《回霍经制启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回霍经制启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216699")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216699_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216699'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216699'>委迹家山，常迂轩骑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216699_comment'></div>剖符江介，复枉缄书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216699_comment'></div>荷眷义之不遗，非衰迟之能称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216699_comment'></div>伏惟某官材猷敏济，志节刚方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216699_comment'></div>夙殚稽古之勤，力传家法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216699_comment'></div>遂展佐时之略，自结主知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216699_comment'></div>中外践更，猷为备著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216699_comment'></div>适此干戈之后，孰先赋敛之图？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216699_comment'></div>凋瘵未苏，调度多阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216699_comment'></div>惟爱民若赤子，故知取而不伤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216699_comment'></div>若言利析秋毫，则虽多而何补？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216699_comment'></div>辍从卿月，暂佐使星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216699_comment'></div>聊烦规画之行，即有超升之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216699_comment'></div>旌麾在望，款谒尚遥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216699_comment'></div>条教所依，瞻言徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216699_comment'></div>尚勉加于调摄，益顺导于绥将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216699_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1216699_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年1月</a>　在建康，正月，有奏状。作品：《奏乞蠲免回易钱状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216593?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞蠲免回易钱状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216593")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216593'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216593'>右，臣伏见户部总领司拘催回易四库人户借欠钱一百一十七万贯有零，内本钱九十三万贯有零，息钱二十三万贯有零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216593_comment'></div>今已通催到本息钱八十三万贯有零，其未纳钱共计三十三万贯有零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216593_comment'></div>契勘上件钱，初缘都督府委户部措置，分设四库，支降官本，委官专监，召募经纪人请领斡运，岁取其息五分四毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216593_comment'></div>法行之初，官吏观望，但欲俵散数多，更不选择人户有无行止、家业，及责取抵保，便行给付。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216593_comment'></div>多是市井浮浪之人，一户有请至二十万贯，其人又各加倍增利，转相借贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216593_comment'></div>元约随监官立界，以三年为限，旋悟其失，才及半年，却行拘收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216593_comment'></div>元非一顿给付见钱，半是金银、盐钞及刘光世献纳物帛积尺、故衣杂物等准折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216593_comment'></div>日月先后，给降不齐，便自投募之日，计日理息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216593_comment'></div>虽有请到官钱，发泄未尽，及造屋置铺、开张门面、般担穿排、脚乘糜费之类，破费已多，未及经营偿补，遽已住罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216593_comment'></div>兼本府累经大火，其转息人户亦有横遭焚荡，损陷生业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216593_comment'></div>昨自去年九月内住罢，总领司据逐户见在钱本物货，已尽数收簇在官，其斡运未还及转借散在人头等钱，接续拘催。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216593_comment'></div>至今年七月内，准尚书省劄子，行下枢密副使行府所申，委自本府将逐户斡运未还钱选委使臣前去根逐拘收，其占压物货责限变转送纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216593_comment'></div>其间多是虚桩妄指，递相干连，均摊分擘，讼诉纷错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216593_comment'></div>兼有不合追理钱数，有司未曾出豁，期限既迫，不免日监夜禁，累然禁锢，荷项相连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216593_comment'></div>近蒙朝廷察见，再准尚书省劄子，据实系元立文约关借官钱经纪人正身及保人监催，其馀干连人等并疏出，责限在外，出豁送纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216593_comment'></div>及准户部总领司牒，坐到都省批状指挥，未曾责定日限人展限一季，本府依应施行，至九月二十三日已限满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216593_comment'></div>臣窃惟出大农钱以啖豪右，诱误贪民，均分其息，此正前日青苗、市易有司商利之过，然犹是一顿见钱，取息不过二分，明立期限，而议者谓之放债取利，至今以为口实，元祐初首先罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216593_comment'></div>昨都督府乃缘一时军兴，户部遽复举行，而兼以杂物，取息至于五分四毫，比之前日，实多一倍以上，初以三年为限，半年遽辄住罢，殆近罔民，其失盖又过于前比，岂陛下散利薄征、惠安斯民之意哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216593_comment'></div>窃详自来民间有利债负，于法皆不当受理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216593_comment'></div>而自兵兴以来，烧劫地分官私欠负，累经赦宥，例多倚阁除放，不应此钱独不少贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216593_comment'></div>所有先支降官本钱九十三万贯，今通本息已纳过八十三万贯，止欠一十万馀贯，见有使臣根逐未到，及合变卖物货钱，约计一十二万贯有零，自可了足有馀，不至失陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216593_comment'></div>其见欠钱三十三万贯，除上项一十二万贯有零，止是有二十一万馀贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216593_comment'></div>若理元约四分二釐息钱，九十三万贯半年只合纳一十八万九千贯有零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216593_comment'></div>内却有官司非理纽算，如请钱未足，便自投募日预行计息，及九月十三日住罢，而虚理息直至十一月三十日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216593_comment'></div>元约岁理息四分二釐，后改为月理，多取其八釐四毫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216593_comment'></div>元约四分息钱外，斡运钱更纳二釐充税钱，出历免其沿路商税，后来却重叠再行收理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216593_comment'></div>元折物货已经估价还官，次年再估扑，低小亏折元数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216593_comment'></div>与盐钞在场待次经隔日分，市易务后来自请变卖得息，不分已前日数拨还，却尽拘收，等五项，皆是不合追纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216593_comment'></div>若行出豁，则自馀正欠息钱止是十万馀贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216593_comment'></div>而监官住罢俸给，拘系坐待人户一百二十馀人，监督在官，经今一年，再迫冬寒，无由了绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216593_comment'></div>臣忝与提领总领司事，本府又系催理官司，不敢隐默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216593_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降睿旨，应见欠人户，委自臣与户部总领司官同共看详，先将前件五项定验诣实，改正出豁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216593_comment'></div>纽见的实合纳钱数，将使臣根逐及合变卖物产依旧催理填足九十三万贯正本外，其馀正欠及转欠人，通同本息，别责宽限料次送纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216593_comment'></div>实经焚烧损折，委是贫乏无以出备之人，并特与除放，昭示德意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216593_comment'></div>明著有司之失，使小人通知非出朝廷，其于今日政事宽大忠厚之美不为无补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1216593_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1216593_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1216593_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1216593'>〔贴黄〕臣契勘见监正欠及转欠人户共一百二十馀人，目今财产有无不同，若逐户下各计本息追纳，理难齐一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1216593_comment'></div>惟有先将见纳到钱通同本息还足元本钱九十三万贯有零外，其馀或本或息，各逐户下财产，委自守臣等验实保明，有则宽限催理，无则除放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1216593_comment'></div>庶几可以了绝，不致虚延岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1216593_comment'></div>伏乞睿察<span class='inlineComment2'>（《石林奏议》卷八。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1216593_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1216593'>息钱止：原缺，据汲古阁本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1216593_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　仲春，与马参议同游蒋山，有诗唱和。作品：《次韵马参议同游蒋山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《再次韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《三次韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《四次韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526643?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵马参议同游蒋山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526643")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526643'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526643'>华屋惊随劫火飞，江山空自绕邦圻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526643'>灵踪可便超千载，妙解谁从寄一微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526643'>著屐尚堪穷碧落，据床聊伴俯清辉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526643'>追寻会识关心处，未怪衰翁苦忆归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526643'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526643_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526644?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526644")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526644'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526644'>颓垣败屋落花飞，草草春光亦故圻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526644'>但爱野塘输渌净，不知风景转清微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526644'>帐空尚忆猿惊晓，基废犹传凤览辉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526644'>女几自无平贼意，坐来休笑久忘归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526644'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526644_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526645?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526645")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526645_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526645'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526645'>荒林寂寂鸟飞飞，旧事那容数一圻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526645'>山色自怜云泱莽，暮寒犹作雨霏微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526645'>谈馀故喜珠<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作舌）</span>仍在，境胜端知玉有辉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526645'>问取塔中黄面老，此生<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作身）</span>何处是真归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526645'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526645_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526646")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526646'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526646'>雨厌残云暝不飞，乱红犹欲点春圻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526646'>蒋陵路绝人谁到，萧寺庭荒迹已微。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526646_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在建康，仲春，蔡子因相过，留连数月，石林有酬唱诗四首。作品：《蔡子因相过留逾月》<span
