id='poem_title_80325_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_80325'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_80325'>经年不踏斜桥路。青山试问谁为主。<div id='poem_sentence_0_80325_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_80325'>密叶转回风。寒泉落半空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_80325_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_80325'>此间无限兴。可便荒三径。<div id='poem_sentence_2_80325_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_80325'>明日下扁舟。沧波莫浪游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_80325_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_80325'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_80325_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年6月</a>　在建康，六月，有《赐砚铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216769' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216769' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216769?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐砚铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216769")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216769_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216769'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216769'>绍兴己未六月，臣某待罪建康之明年，皇帝以所尝御砚赐臣某，谨再拜稽首而为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216769'>咸池之渊，奎钩所直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216769_comment'></div>发为天地，号令攸出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216769_comment'></div>惟泰山云，肤寸万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216769_comment'></div>帝泽之储，而臣之藏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1216769_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在建康，夏，有与秦桧论买耕牛书。作品：《又与秦相公书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在建康，夏，有奏状。作品：《奏措置买牛租赁与民耕种利害状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏措置买牛租赁与民耕种利害状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216606")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216606'>右，臣近准御前金字牌封下尚书省劄子，以淮西及本路等处牛疫死损，奉圣旨专委臣措置，取拨常平所管诸色钱物，委官于出产耕牛去处广行收买，令人户租赁，应副耕种，务要不失农时，仍许从长酌度，随宜施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216606_comment'></div>除已即时行下所部州军，取会各管常平钱物数目，委自逐州选差官就近体访出产去处，计会收买外，仍委本府倚郭两县知县并职官、本司属官各一员，于本府界内询究阙牛人户见各如何处置接济耕种；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216606_comment'></div>并下管内五县，取责今年内开剥过倒死牛比较分数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216606_comment'></div>据申，今年倒死牛共约计一千二百馀头，比去年计多两倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216606_comment'></div>系疫死之数，未知一路多寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216606_comment'></div>今年正月以后，节次疫气流行，有一家三五头并皆倒死，一家十头全无死损者，各自不等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216606_comment'></div>其牛疫之家、无力下户，多是于无死损有馀之家通那租赁，或于客贩处连合财本就近收买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216606_comment'></div>其有力上户即于两浙温、台、明、越等州兴贩归乡耕种，或租赁与人，有无相通，粗已耕垦，趁种早禾了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216606_comment'></div>惟有二麦收刈后合重行耕犁，再种晚禾，今已将毕，约至六月终周遍，亦且依前措置，止是阙少钱本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216606_comment'></div>契勘牛疫路分，自湖南北直至淮西，悉皆被害，其出产路分不过二广、两浙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216606_comment'></div>二广路远，决不可往，两浙虽有，前四州窃虑所馀不多，若诸路并差官前去争买，农民乘时邀价，必难多致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216606_comment'></div>纵有，至速亦须一月馀日方可到本路州军，即于晚稻耕种已不及用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216606_comment'></div>兼牛畏暑，不能行远，两浙经隔程途，若远处多是船载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216606_comment'></div>其间卖牛人户弊倖不一，所差官未必尽能辩认，或因而通同作过，却致不堪使用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216606_comment'></div>兼牛非农人不能究知水草饲养之方，在路别无人部押照管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216606_comment'></div>既到地头州军，须是召人情愿租赁，若不堪使用，或农畏惮倒死备偿，不敢与官中交易，即难以抑配，不免却有空闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216606_comment'></div>数目既多，日久因循死损，非独民间不受实利，兼枉有失陷官钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216606_comment'></div>伏睹绍圣常平免役令，灾伤放税七分以上，并不及七分第四等以下户乏种食者，有结保借贷，给限一年，随税送纳免息之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216606_comment'></div>今来耕牛与种食事体相类，采访民言，若官司各随逐州目今牛价，许令民间不限等第头数，依种食法结保借钱，或三两户共借一头，各令任便，或于本乡村有馀之家，或于隔路出产去处，自行计置收买，应副使用，亦限一年，免息随税还纳元本，则官无差官道路饲养之劳，民心无畏避死损备偿之扰，各得良牛，及时使用，一切弊倖，更不须关防，委是公私两便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216606_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降睿旨，下有司相度，如可采取，即乞速赐行下，以凭遵守施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216606_comment'></div>臣遵奉从长酌度，随宜指挥，行下本路州军，一面令出榜晓谕，召人于所属结保投状，依借贷种法，听候朝廷指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216606_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216606_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1216606_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在建康，秋，有祈晴文。作品：《祈晴诸庙文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　是年，在建康，有文。作品：《书高居实集后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216745' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216745' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216745?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书高居实集后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216745")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216745_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216745'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216745'>元祐末，余与居实同举进士，试春官，数往来舅氏晁无咎家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216745_comment'></div>时张文潜为右史，二公一时后进所推尊，每得居实文，皆击节称赏不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216745_comment'></div>居实试别头，文潜适主文，居实果擢第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216745_comment'></div>胡右丞完夫见其所赋《主圣臣直》，声言于众曰：「此岂赋耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216745_comment'></div>殆有韵《陆宣公奏议》尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216745_comment'></div>时国论颇厌文弊，将复唐宏辞科，居实首中选，复为第一，于是名称日闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216745_comment'></div>已而坐上书排党论，久不得调，卒邑邑不得志以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216745_comment'></div>余后不复见居实，然间有出其所为诗文者，每见每奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216745_comment'></div>始，天下名文章称无咎、文潜，曰「晁张」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216745_comment'></div>无咎雄健峻拔，笔力欲挽千钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216745_comment'></div>文潜容衍靖深，独若不得已于言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216745_comment'></div>二公各以所长名家，不以相易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216745_comment'></div>而居实之文，气和而思远，言约而理畅，超然常出事物之外，而观者每有馀味，故人以为似文潜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216745_comment'></div>绍兴己未，余守建康，居实之子绍持其遗文一编相示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216745_comment'></div>兵火散亡之馀，所存盖十一，览之太息，追数往游，俯仰如前日事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216745_comment'></div>居实之志既不得伸于生前，著后世者惟其文字，又不幸不得尽传于后，为可哀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216745_comment'></div>乃书其后归之，且以嘉绍之能不坠其业也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1216745_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　是年，在建康，有与秦桧书。作品：《与秦相公论臧梓狱事书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216719' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216719' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216719?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与秦相公论臧梓狱事书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216719")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216719_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216719'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216719'>某顿首再拜，上启仆射相公钧席：连雨，尚有馀寒，即日伏惟钧候万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216719_comment'></div>某近尝托徐度司封上记，必获□□拙，蒙庇粗遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216719_comment'></div>臧梓事竟烦庙议，移狱公朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216719_comment'></div>正名分，严赏罚，固一民不可使有冤，不得不尽其情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216719_comment'></div>但无状，仰误委寄，愧悚无以自容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216719_comment'></div>已具奏乞降指挥，遣一御史按验，然区区之私，犹欲少伸于相公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216719_comment'></div>近世毁誉，常患不出公道，人自为党，更相与夺，故名实倒植，而赏罚随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216719_comment'></div>此有识者扼腕愤叹，欲正而不得者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216719_comment'></div>梓前为寿昌令，以治状为台臣所荐，得改官堂除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216719_comment'></div>近以公事决责宣抚司军兵，自言不畏强御，故为之类者亦交口称誉，其为人宜当如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216719_comment'></div>而所犯狼籍，殆非他赃吏可比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216719_comment'></div>有司具狱，略见入己者为钱九千贯、银五百五十两、绢二百匹、绵九百两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216719_comment'></div>又去官后，犹盗库钱三百五十缗、官木二十条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216719_comment'></div>此其證佐，来历分明，不可掩覆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216719_comment'></div>其馀牵连杂见，尚数千缗，与因丧取之部民者，皆未暇问也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216719_comment'></div>不识为长吏者，从前日虚名庇之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216719_comment'></div>正今日隐恶劾之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216719_comment'></div>以律言，则监临有犯，知而不举，减罪三等；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216719_comment'></div>以绍兴五年敕言，县有罪，监司按举，而州不举，减罪人罪五等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216719_comment'></div>就其间一事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216719_comment'></div>某去岁到官之初，首论民间疾苦，乞减内藏库和买税七分，折纳见钱□□贯省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216719_comment'></div>蒙上开纳，亟以金字牌报可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216719_comment'></div>德意始传，阖境欢呼，几至流泪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216719_comment'></div>倚郭上元令曾恢违戾，多折至八贯省，而不入己，去冬因民讼，即奏削免勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216719_comment'></div>梓多取乃至十贯四百省，而盗其五贯四百省入己，朱钞具在，此宣抚司首所奏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216719_comment'></div>若以宣抚司不应奏，本府亦纵而不治，曾恢他日被罪，披诉朝廷，覆视得实，或谏官御史风闻有言，则将何辞以对？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216719_comment'></div>非特法不容，人固不相容也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216719_comment'></div>梓先决宣抚司军兵，本自非理，正缓急欲藉口自解免，宣抚司军兵堕其计中，遽越职论奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216719_comment'></div>自彼之失，何预本府事，而自以为嫌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216719_comment'></div>某所以于遣官体究得实之后，判然不疑，力伐其谋，一以法令从事，庶几忝以大臣守陪都，稍异流俗，为天下发一大奸，少正群儿妄誉误赏之弊，或可上补朝廷公论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216719_comment'></div>岂意罪人尚敢伸其说，宣抚司盖与并肩而立，何所重轻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216719_comment'></div>自到任，此惟齐以礼法，秋毫不相假借，故能各守其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216719_comment'></div>只如近者朝旨相度修战船，恐为民病，尚不能从，况其甚者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216719_comment'></div>流落半世，正坐无所俯仰，今老得一州，乃观望同列诬人功罪于行阙数百里之内，不顾旁观，自丧晚节，意欲何为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216719_comment'></div>相公见知有素，必未期之至此，自是奇蹇招感，所至皆然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1216719_comment'></div>每欲速还山林，不敢一日为苟安计，初若畏懦可笑，今当信其非伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1216719_comment'></div>无缘晤省，窃恃眷予，烦喋不觉盈纸，悚息无已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1216719_comment'></div>尚幸矜察，检会前奏，早赐从允，不胜恳祷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1216719_comment'></div>馀祈上为兴运倍加保重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1216719_comment'></div>谨上状，不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1216719_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年1月</a>　在建康任，正月，以疾病上章再乞宫观。作品：《第二次乞宫观第一状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>第二次乞宫观第一状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216514")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216514'>右，臣昨蒙误恩，久叨寄任，尸素无补，旷戾日多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216514_comment'></div>去岁尝具奏乞就闲秩，伏蒙曲降诏书，未赐俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216514_comment'></div>蝼蚁微生，上勤洪造，徬徨黾勉，又已踰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216514_comment'></div>伏念臣犬马之齿六十有四，衰羸多病，每岁有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216514_comment'></div>自去年十月以来，旧苦肺气屡作，至今尚未平复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216514_comment'></div>兵民所会，事责非轻，若更迁延冒居，必速咎悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216514_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特赐哀怜，除臣依旧在外一宫观差遣，任便居住，庶几休养残骸，粗全晚节，不至重干清议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1216514_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年2月</a>　在建康任，二月，上乞宫观《第二状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年2月12日</a>　在建康任，二月十二日，作《书明皇吹箫图后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216746' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216746' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216746?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书明皇吹箫图后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年2月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216746")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216746_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216746'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216746'>此周昉画，家旧有南唐摹本，笔迹如屈发，今亡之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216746_comment'></div>其傍有海棠一株，宁王坐其左，执板者黄幡绰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216746_comment'></div>此本出梁仲谟家，仅存其五六尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216746_comment'></div>明皇末年，暇时自适，但如画中，亦安得有马嵬事耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216746_comment'></div>绍兴庚申二月十二日，久阴初晴，为山亭，与何彦发同观。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1216746_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年2月22日</a>　在建康任，二月二十二日，进官一秩，由左中大夫升左大中大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年2月</a>　在建康任，二月，有辞免左大中大夫奏状。作品：《辞免左大中大夫状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216517?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免左大中大夫状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216517")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216517'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216517'>右，臣今月初十日，准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨与转一官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216517_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知攸措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216517_comment'></div>伏念臣衰病无能，过叨剧任，徒淹岁月，莫效寸劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216517_comment'></div>方自力求闲秩，冀逃官谤，未知何名，复冒此赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216517_comment'></div>苟怀贪得，必致烦言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216517_comment'></div>欲望圣慈俯察危诚，收还成命，使少安于愚分，庶无累于公朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216517_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1216517_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年2月</a>　在建康任，二月，有辞免左大中大夫札子。作品：《辞免左大中大夫札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免左大中大夫劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216498")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216498'>臣近者愿解留都，已屡干渊听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216498_comment'></div>今复辞误宠，仰犯天诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216498_comment'></div>退省徬徨，已甘窜殛，迫于私义，尚敢缕陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216498_comment'></div>感惧交并，陨越无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216498_comment'></div>臣闻先王诏爵制禄，皆有常法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216498_comment'></div>既已命之，则于三年考绩，随其幽明而为之黜陟，人无得容其私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216498_comment'></div>若加命进秩，则必职事之外别有殊功异能，然后为非常之赐，谓之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216498_comment'></div>故文武造周，能锡有功诸侯，则诗人美之，作为《彤弓》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216498_comment'></div>简王无因而褒鲁成公，则《春秋》变文而书曰「天子使召伯来赐公命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216498_comment'></div>伏念臣自到任以来，行将二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216498_comment'></div>当新疆初复，疲民始安之际，虽愿竭情尽瘁，少图报效，而材力有限，病衰相仍，上无尺寸可裨朝廷，下无毫发可及闾里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216498_comment'></div>臣之自审，岂不甚明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216498_comment'></div>陛下天地涵容，纵以奉法循理、龊龊廉谨，阔略细过，使得容身而去，固已万幸，岂可更冒异恩，妄叨非据？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216498_comment'></div>窃惟方今外难粗宁，而四方万里之远，百官庶府之事，多尚废阙，正须内外夙夜协心，相与共济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216498_comment'></div>若藩镇近臣不能上体圣志，犹务贪得，此臣所以尤恐惧震惕而不敢当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216498_comment'></div>伏望圣慈洞察肺肝，特赐寝罢，使区区微臣，得以俯全一介之守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216498_comment'></div>则天下稍知分义者，孰不人人兴起，皆有乐事劝功之意，庶亦不为无补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1216498_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年2月</a>　在建康任，二月，有谢转官启。作品：《转大中大夫谢执政启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216703' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216703' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216703?labeling=true' target='_blank'>转大中大夫谢执政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216703")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216703_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216703'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216703'>量能授官，盖先王用人之本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216703_comment'></div>见得思义，亦君子行己之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216703_comment'></div>仰累公朝，退惭本意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216703_comment'></div>伏念某受材不敏，涉世多艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216703_comment'></div>方强仕之年，固已自投于闲散；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216703_comment'></div>岂既衰之后，反求贪得于须臾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216703_comment'></div>况风波荐履于畏涂，而荆棘亲逢于晚岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216703_comment'></div>正使捐躯原野，未偿廪食之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216703_comment'></div>矧惟服力簿书，何补事劳之实？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216703_comment'></div>取非其有，人且谓何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216703_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官拔茅与其汇征，采菲不以下体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216703_comment'></div>方流言窃诋，独深亮其无他；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216703_comment'></div>逮告疾引归，复挽留而不释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216703_comment'></div>矜其迟暮，借以宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216703_comment'></div>不称所蒙，岂曰子衣之安吉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216703_comment'></div>未知为报，徒怀我马之虺隤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216703_comment'></div>震惧靡宁，铭藏曷已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216703_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1216703_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年2月</a>　在建康任，二月，建康府学竣工，有纪文。作品：《府学记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216763' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216763' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216763?labeling=true' target='_blank'>府学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216763")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216763_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216763'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216763'>先王以武定天下，必以文终之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216763_comment'></div>《江汉》，宣王南征之诗也，其言甲兵车马之盛备矣，至于末乃曰「矢其文德，洽此四国」，治道岂不有本末乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216763_comment'></div>卫灵公问陈，子曰：「俎豆之事则尝闻之矣，军旅之事未之学也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216763_comment'></div>子岂以军旅为不足学哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216763_comment'></div>以为知所以为俎豆，则军旅无不可为，虽曰我战则克可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216763_comment'></div>汉高帝悉定楚地，独鲁不下，引天下兵欲屠之，鲁中诸儒尚讲诵习礼，弦歌之音不绝，遂不敢加，而待其服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216763_comment'></div>大道之行，固有不期然而然者，孰谓鲁诸儒而能折高帝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216763_comment'></div>推而上之，舜舞干羽，而有苗格，谓之「诞敷文德」，无足怪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216763_comment'></div>盖礼义之在人心，莫不皆有，苟未至于绝灭，不幸丧失，虽至于犯上作乱，徐返其本，亦必悔而知变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216763_comment'></div>善为治者，可待之以变，而得所向，不可期之以绝灭而终不返，则文德其可一日废于天下乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216763_comment'></div>学校固理义之所从出，而斯文之所先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216763_comment'></div>建康领江左八州之地，于东南为大都会，异时文献甲于他方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216763_comment'></div>旧有学在州之巽隅，更罹兵火，城郭鞠为丘墟，独学宫岿然仅存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216763_comment'></div>颓垣败壁，毁压相藉，生徒奔散，博士倚席不讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216763_comment'></div>绍兴二年，某始以安抚大使分镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216763_comment'></div>方时自淮以北，裂为盗区，蜂屯豕突，鼙鼓相闻，盖欲葺而未暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216763_comment'></div>后七年，大驾还钱塘，诏以建康为留都，蒙恩复畀居守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216763_comment'></div>视事之明年，辑宁荒残，流亡稍复，民亦安业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216763_comment'></div>于是喟然曰：可以有事于学矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216763_comment'></div>乃命其属，因旧址，尽彻而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216763_comment'></div>起己未孟冬，讫庚申仲春，凡五月，为屋百二十有五间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216763_comment'></div>辟其南向，以面秦淮，增斥讲肆，列置斋庐，高明爽垲，固有加于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216763_comment'></div>不侈不陋，下及庖圊，罔不毕具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216763_comment'></div>既又作小学于大门之东，复命有司诹典礼簿，正祭器，作新冕黼，皆中程式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216763_comment'></div>覈其田之在属邑，募民耕者千九百十五亩，岁入其赋，为米若豆与麦五百四十斛有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216763_comment'></div>坊之得自酤者三区，岁入其课，为钱百八十万有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216763_comment'></div>地之占府城，得佃而居者八十有五所，岁入其租，为钱六百七十五万有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216763_comment'></div>各为图籍，以时输之，凡廪给之费，无有欺匿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216763_comment'></div>乃以上丁，释奠于先圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216763_comment'></div>前期，率郡执事斋于两序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216763_comment'></div>盖诸生无不从视涤，省牲惟谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216763_comment'></div>昧旦夙兴，笾豆在列，肴酒静嘉，币篚洁严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216763_comment'></div>史告时至，以次就位，正笏垂绅，佩玉铿锵，降登伏兴，卒事无违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216763_comment'></div>礼成受釐，哜爵于阼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216763_comment'></div>观者数百人，皆骇其所未见，无不太息感动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1216763_comment'></div>退而揖所与祭者而告曰：「呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1216763_comment'></div>子衿之作，郑人之所耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1216763_comment'></div>是不知在郑何公，然传载然明欲毁乡校，子产不可，则当子产时，乡校盖复存，是郑之学未尝终废，有子产则能兴之焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1216763_comment'></div>四方用兵踰十年，学校之列于郡国者，其亡与存，我不敢知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1216763_comment'></div>惟天子以仁孝勤俭治天下，克复大业，愿与中外休息，还之承平者，盖终食不忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1216763_comment'></div>上帝监观，亦既归我河南之地，兵革渐息，惟舜、宣王之德，于兹将兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1216763_comment'></div>吾邦号陪都，视定鼎郏鄏，实为宗周，是亦风化之首，其复有学自今始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1216763_comment'></div>肉食者其可不推子产之为郑，以求先圣眷眷俎豆之意，相与先后辅成吾君之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1216763_comment'></div>布衣韦带亦必有宏达英伟之士，拔于草莱，接踵继起，由此而出，以共济一世者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1216763_comment'></div>子大夫尚勉之」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1216763_comment'></div>皆曰「唯」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1216763_comment'></div>遂为记，刻之石，后来者其有考焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1216763_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年2月</a>　在建康任，二月，有奏札。作品：《奏乞府学添差教授状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏乞府学不许官司指佔状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216608' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216608' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216608?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞府学添差教授状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216608")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216608'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216608'>右，臣近重建本府学舍毕工，访闻西北流寓士子皆欲前来听读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216608_comment'></div>旧止有教授一员，窃虑人众，训导不能遍及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216608_comment'></div>伏见临安府府学日近曾奏请添差教授一员，特蒙朝廷施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216608_comment'></div>今来本府事体一同，欲望圣慈依例更特添差教授一员，以幸学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216608_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216608_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1216608_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216609?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞府学不许官司指占状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216609")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216609'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216609'>右，臣窃见本府学舍，兵火之馀，虽仅免焚荡，然所存屋宇，倾摧过半，四方流寓学者多至本府，皆无所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216609_comment'></div>臣于去年冬，因根治学粮欺隐，得其羡钱，并积聚在官竹木等，委官重行盖造，今已毕工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216609_comment'></div>共一百四十五间，创置什物略备，稍可安养士人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216609_comment'></div>契勘兵兴以来，州郡学校多为官司指占作廨舍局务，其什物亦皆为人借换窃取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216609_comment'></div>今者兵革渐息，陛下留意文治，未尝一日暂忘科举取士，不废祖宗之旧，则教养之地，有司所宜共承德意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216609_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降指挥，应今后官司，并不许指占居住，其什物亦不得擅有假借，违者重坐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216609_comment'></div>庶几人知儆劝，复见礼义之化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216609_comment'></div>并以风示遐迩，逆折暴横彊犷之心，使知所畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216609_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216609_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216609_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1216609'>〔贴黄〕臣今来所乞，系干风教，如蒙圣慈采取，所有诸路州军学校亦乞一例施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216609_comment'></div>伏乞睿察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1216609_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年3月</a>　在建康任，三月，有诗寄徐度。作品：《徐惇立罢吏部郎官出守天台待次卞山旧居因寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526655' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526655?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徐惇立罢吏部郎官出守天台待次卞山旧居因寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526655")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526655_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526655'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526655'>嵇康不作绝交书，出处萧然两裕如。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526655'>锦帐不妨游省户，草堂还得赋郊居。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526655'>倾崖溅水青云上，夹道轻阴落絮馀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526655'>亦<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作肯）</span>记旧游聊待我，未须催<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>驾赤城车。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526655'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526655'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_526655_0'>⑴ 原作摧，据影宋本、四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526655_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年3月19日</a>　在建康任，三月十九日，上乞宫观《第三状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年4月</a>　在建康任，四月，奏荐部属李朝正。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年5月13日</a>　在建康任，五月十三日，奏扩建行宫，不从。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年5月</a>　在建康任，五月十三日前后，有奏议。作品：《宫室议》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216599' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216599' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216599?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宫室议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216599")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216599_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216599'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216599'>议曰：臣闻古者帝王宫室之制，不尽载于经，而略见于《周官》与《礼》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216599_comment'></div>为门者五，为朝者三，为寝与宫者皆六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216599_comment'></div>所谓五门者，曰皋门、曰库门、曰雉门、曰应门、曰路门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216599_comment'></div>皋门，先儒谓王城之门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216599_comment'></div>库门次之宗庙社稷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216599_comment'></div>其内雉门，王宫之门，故旁设两观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216599_comment'></div>此五门之别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216599_comment'></div>所谓三朝者，曰外朝、曰内朝、曰燕朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216599_comment'></div>《周官》朝士掌外朝之法，凡公卿大夫、公侯伯子男、三公，皆有定位，是谓外朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216599_comment'></div>司士掌朝仪之位，三公、卿大夫、王族、故士、虎士、太仆、太右皆有定位，是谓内朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216599_comment'></div>太仆掌王之服位，王视治朝，则前正位而退，入亦如之，是谓燕朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216599_comment'></div>《礼·玉藻》言王朝服以日视朝于内朝，退适内寝听政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216599_comment'></div>先儒谓外朝在库门之外，凡国有大事，致万民而询焉，则御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216599_comment'></div>内朝在路门之外，凡日视朝见群臣则御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216599_comment'></div>燕朝在路门之内，凡日退而听政则御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216599_comment'></div>此三朝之别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216599_comment'></div>所谓六寝六宫者，先儒以《周官》「宫人掌王之六寝之脩」为言，谓路寝一、小寝五，盖在路门之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216599_comment'></div>而六宫王后之居又在其后，视王之六寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216599_comment'></div>此六寝、六宫之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216599_comment'></div>秦汉而下，沿革不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216599_comment'></div>即唐之近制考之，唐以宣政为前殿，谓之正衙，即周之内朝也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216599_comment'></div>以紫宸为便殿，谓之閤，即周之燕朝也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216599_comment'></div>而无外朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216599_comment'></div>日御正衙见群臣，谓之常参。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216599_comment'></div>朔望荐食诸陵寝，有思慕之心，不能临前殿，即唤仗入紫宸，谓之入閤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216599_comment'></div>至五代，其礼寖废，常参不复日见群臣，惟大臣一朝便殿而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216599_comment'></div>后唐明宗即位，始诏百官五日一随宰相入见便殿，谓之起居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216599_comment'></div>本朝因唐之旧，参酌古制，更为增损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216599_comment'></div>今汴都南薰、朱雀门宜为古之雉门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216599_comment'></div>以大庆殿为外朝，故岁旦大朝会则御之，而其门即应门也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216599_comment'></div>以文德殿为内朝，故月朔合六参官入见则御之，而其门即路门也，谓之过殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216599_comment'></div>其旁设东西閤门，则仿唐制以紫宸、垂拱为閤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216599_comment'></div>遇朔不过殿，则唤仗入閤，而御紫宸，与望及五日百官一起居皆御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216599_comment'></div>以垂拱为燕朝，则日御以听政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216599_comment'></div>盖相仍唐室旧内增修，不得不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1216599_comment'></div>今陛下既以建康为别都，则视周洛邑与汴京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1216599_comment'></div>岁大朝会见百官御大庆，月朔过殿御文德，望与六参御紫宸，日御垂拱，此四殿有不可阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1216599_comment'></div>而忌前不坐垂拱，与吏部引见选人、军头司呈试武艺等，本朝所增盖又有崇政后殿，讲筵有迩英殿，亦不可废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1216599_comment'></div>此典礼所在，将以垂后经远，固宜参备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1216599_comment'></div>端门亦当增为三门，以正天子之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1216599_comment'></div>则朝群臣，莅四夷，赋政出令，行礼正名，上拟洛邑，次不失祖宗之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1216599_comment'></div>若夫高下之度、广狭之数，则先王初不为定制，各视时而为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1216599_comment'></div>商之重屋，堂高三尺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1216599_comment'></div>周之明堂，堂高九尺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1216599_comment'></div>若禹卑宫室，则夏之世室，其高一尺而已，其高下固不等也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1216599_comment'></div>周之路门不容乘车之五个，为丈有六尺五寸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1216599_comment'></div>应门二彻三个，为二丈四尺，其广狭固不同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1216599_comment'></div>恭惟陛下以宽仁信兆民，以惇朴先天下，圣志固自有定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1216599_comment'></div>今宫城之内，其地有限，若有司推明德意，但取典礼所不可废者，而不为观美，则与其大而有阙，不若狭而能备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1216599_comment'></div>惟六寝、六宫在内中，《周礼》既不详，祖宗成法见于汴京者，因时便宜，当出圣裁，非臣所敢及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1216599_comment'></div>谨昧死上《宫室议》，伏惟陛下垂意采择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1216599_comment'></div>臣谨议。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1216599'></div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1216599_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年5月</a>　在建康任，五月十三日前后，有奏札。作品：《奏缴行宫图并宫室议札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏营葺行宫制度画一札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏论行宫防守札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《堂白营葺行宫画一札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏缴行宫图并宫室议劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216600")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216600'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216600'>臣近准尚书省劄子，备奉圣旨，以本府行宫昨缘临时修盖，不如法，及百司等屋宇，亦因旋行修造，致多苟简，专委臣相度措置，立定规摹，画图缴进，逐旋如法营葺，务要可以经久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216600_comment'></div>臣衰陋不材，误蒙重寄，实非所能任，承命震恐，不敢辄辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216600_comment'></div>退考之古昔，周文武既定都于丰，谓之宗周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216600_comment'></div>至成王欲宅洛邑，乃复营之，谓之成周，亦曰东都，以为四方道里远近之中，使朝觐贡赋取均焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216600_comment'></div>及宣王遭犬戎之难，会诸侯于东都，选车马、备器械，因还以居，周遂中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216600_comment'></div>则有正都，有别都，自周而然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216600_comment'></div>晋重耳败楚城濮，迨齐小白正天下之义，合诸侯于践土，周襄王巡守临之，《春秋》书「天王狩于河阳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216600_comment'></div>鲁僖公朝于王所，而《左氏》记「重耳作王宫于衡雍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216600_comment'></div>则天子巡守，亦作宫焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216600_comment'></div>然《洛诰》称「用牲于郊，乃社于新邑」，有郊有社，庶邦冢君皆在，则别都之礼宜略与正都同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216600_comment'></div>而巡守之宫，止以朝见方岳，则宜从约也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216600_comment'></div>今陛下巡幸东南，临安盖巡守之宫，而以建康为别都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216600_comment'></div>则车驾未即还汴，建康行宫受朝四方，赋政出令，视临安宜有当增备者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216600_comment'></div>孔子颂禹之德曰「卑宫室而尽力乎沟洫」，然则宫室虽在所备，要以不侈大而卑为美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216600_comment'></div>汉高祖入关，命萧何治未央宫，见其壮丽而怒曰：「天下汹汹，劳苦数岁，成败未可知，是何治宫室过度也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216600_comment'></div>世以高祖为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216600_comment'></div>晋孝武时，宫室弊坏，谢安修之，皆仰模元象，合体宸极，后世讥焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216600_comment'></div>恭惟陛下宏济艰难，圣猷恢远，勤俭之意，天下耸闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216600_comment'></div>臣顷者获侍清光，亲所目击，虽服食器用之间，有臣庶不堪者，陛下皆安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216600_comment'></div>今中原初定，渐图经理，始用成周之制，因时便事，营创别都，以兴王业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216600_comment'></div>臣愚敢不上体圣志，无费财，无妄役，无扰民，参酌古今典礼所必不可阙者，然后为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216600_comment'></div>惟是今宫室地步，昨来营缮禁中，与外庭分擘去处，参差不齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216600_comment'></div>若止据见在地步相度，即偏曲窄小，其合添殿宇官府等难以安排。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216600_comment'></div>若欲参备，以为经远持久之计，则须有禁中空地那融去处，非臣所敢专决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216600_comment'></div>今先次各草立规模，措置画到图二本，各行贴说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216600_comment'></div>并臣参酌古今典礼、沿革制度，撰成《宫室议》一篇，头连在前，同共缴进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216600_comment'></div>伏望圣慈取自睿断，行下付臣，重具定本进呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216600_comment'></div>所有图内增添殿宇官府，移改安排事理，及那融禁中地步丈尺数目，与内外防守利害，合奏禀事，各别具劄子画一开陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216600_comment'></div>臣学术浅陋，思虑不远，闻见不广，无以仰称陛下委使之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216600_comment'></div>尘犯天威，臣无任惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216600_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216600_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1216600'>〔贴黄〕契勘昨来本府营造，拟定图本进呈，蒙差内侍王鉴前来覆视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216600_comment'></div>今事干宫禁内外久远利害，臣所见窃虑未尽未便，欲望圣慈特赐依例差官一员，与臣同共审定，分擘内外地界，取旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1216600_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216601' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216601' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216601?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏营葺行宫制度画一劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216601")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216601_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216601'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216601'>臣遵奉圣训，先次草具到营葺行宫图二本并《宫室议》一篇缴进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216601_comment'></div>所有图内参考古制，所当增添殿宇官府事理，并那融禁中地步丈尺数目，及宫城外门制度，合详具奏禀，今具画一开陈下项：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1216601'>一、《周官》，王国皆旁为三门，此天子之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216601_comment'></div>盖五门皆取正中一门名之，其旁又为两门，通为三门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216601_comment'></div>至雉门为王宫之门，每正月之吉，以垂治象，则又有象魏设于门之左右，谓之两观，亦或谓之阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216601_comment'></div>诸侯则不得备三门，而无两观，故独鲁以周公之赐得有两观，则新作南门与新作雉门及两观，见书于《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216601_comment'></div>今行宫但因建康府旧制为两门，其上增展门屋九间而已，此诸侯之制也，恐非典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216601_comment'></div>今打量旧城两门各阔一丈七尺，其两间相去有地步六丈，若于中间就开一门，即不须改作，可就立三门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216601_comment'></div>门前东西仗舍各有地步，可以增设两观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216601_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1216601'>一、行宫见今有朝殿一所，并两廊屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216601_comment'></div>其朝殿两柱已损烂中空，见行计置修换。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216601_comment'></div>其馀廊屋等并多损漏，逐时八作司不住检计补葺，未尝有虚日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216601_comment'></div>今契勘宫城内地步，东西南北相去各一百九十馀丈，东除去年淮西宣抚使张俊展套新城五十馀丈，南北内教场五十馀丈，皆属禁中，在外东西相去止有九十馀丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216601_comment'></div>南北自朝殿至宫门虽有九十馀丈，其西面却有禁中曲尺侵过地步，除外，南至宫墙止有四十馀丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216601_comment'></div>东面内东门小殿外即是禁中墙，直至旧几筵殿后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216601_comment'></div>其南自旧几筵殿至宫墙亦止有二十八丈五尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216601_comment'></div>今来若以朝殿为正，就移向南为大庆殿，却以其后基地盖紫宸殿，于紫宸殿西通禁中曲尺侵过地内盖垂拱殿，与紫宸殿作一排，其前盖文德殿，即可略仿汴京旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216601_comment'></div>其那融禁中旧曲尺侵过空地西五十馀丈、北三十馀丈，其垂拱殿西止有十馀丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216601_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1216601'>一、内诸司及内藏库、军器库等，中书门下两省，枢密、学士院，职事皆在内庭，汴京并于皇城内建置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216601_comment'></div>其往来通行路，皆有门为限断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216601_comment'></div>其与禁中相接处，非隔殿宇，则为行廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216601_comment'></div>今行宫除内藏库等散于四旁隙地建造，各不相连接外，其御厨、御药院、翰林司、入内内侍、讲筵所等，并分设于朝殿中门外两廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216601_comment'></div>两省、枢密同为一省，与学士院并在外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216601_comment'></div>皆是一时权宜之制，其通行路处并无别门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216601_comment'></div>内东门小殿东及内教场三面并张俊所展新城，与禁中分隔处止是筑墙，恐不可以示尊严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216601_comment'></div>若依前项措置，正中盖紫宸殿，西盖垂拱殿，接连空地创建行廊一条，直彻内教场东墙，即其南馀剩地可以依仿汴京旧制，减损作两省、枢密、学士院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216601_comment'></div>东面将小殿东旧墙改造行廊一条直彻南面，可以分设御厨等紧要应奉局次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216601_comment'></div>二项不惟可以略备，所添屋宇实外护禁中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216601_comment'></div>却将旧几筵殿基，通南面空地直至宫墙，可以建置内藏库等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216601_comment'></div>凡经由行路，并可度要会处创立别门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216601_comment'></div>其东面改作廊，须那融过禁中六七丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216601_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1216601'>一、祖宗旧制，崇政殿、迩英殿皆在皇城东北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216601_comment'></div>内崇政即讲武殿，盖试习武事之所，应军头引见司呈试武艺，及忌前不坐前殿、吏部引见选人等，皆坐崇政殿，讲筵则坐迩英殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216601_comment'></div>今宫城东北别无空闲地步，其西北内教场射殿逐时引见诸军，乃祖宗讲武之意，若就为崇政殿，即其后空地可以就建迩英殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216601_comment'></div>若其地不可那融，垂拱殿西改造行廊，内禁中亦有空闲地步，可以修建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216601_comment'></div>缘事并属宫禁，非臣所得干预，不敢拟定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1216601_comment'></div>右具进呈，取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1216601_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216602?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论行宫防守劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216602")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216602_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216602'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216602'>臣闻古者作为宫室，上栋下宇，以避风雨，重门击柝，以待暴客，取《易》之《豫》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216602_comment'></div>盖察奸防微、儆戒豫备之道不可不严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216602_comment'></div>故《周官》宫伯为八次八舍，以授王宫士庶子之职事，而宫正掌王宫之戒令纠禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216602_comment'></div>本朝汴京大内、左右掖、东华等门内，皆中通行路，而各为之门，如银台、嘉肃、承天、宣祐、謻门等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216602_comment'></div>其外庭与禁中接连去处，非限以殿宇，则必为行廊，分列班房，以居卫士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216602_comment'></div>其四隅则为巡道，可通往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216602_comment'></div>盖追考古制，祖宗之意深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216602_comment'></div>昨来本府营缮，有司不明大体，自宫城门止有行宫一门并东内门，其馀空闲去处，中夜可以通行，并无几察防守之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216602_comment'></div>其与禁中接连处，但筑墙而已，臣愚以为不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216602_comment'></div>臣今来相度，第一本图增添去处，非止典礼所不可阙，若西以紫宸、垂拱殿一排盖外，其馀空地创造行廊一条，直抵内教场东墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216602_comment'></div>东以内东门小殿东墙改造行廊一条，直抵南面，与大庆殿齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216602_comment'></div>紫宸、垂拱殿前及内东门皆通行路，各以要会去处为门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216602_comment'></div>其改造廊屋分诸司外，馀并布列班房，以严宿卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216602_comment'></div>即禁中四面皆环以殿宇、行廊，尊严深密，略具汴京大内之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216602_comment'></div>惟是内教场直彻城西北角，系在禁中，臣所不得知，不敢窃议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216602_comment'></div>其东面改造行廊之东直抵张俊展套西墙，与禁中接连处虽不为廊，若依臣第一本图措置建造百司屋宇在前，即亦与行廊相等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216602_comment'></div>已各于图内逐项贴说，伏望圣慈少赐省览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216602_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216602_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1216602'>〔贴黄〕臣今拟定合增添殿，且以汴京旧名为称，伏乞睿察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1216602_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216676' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216676' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216676?labeling=true' target='_blank'>堂白营葺行宫画一劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216676")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216676_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216676'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216676'>某见遵奉圣旨措置营葺行宫，已草定具图缴进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216676_comment'></div>所有合增添殿宇官府，及那融侵入禁中地步丈尺，今具画一劄子奏陈外，再具下项：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1216676'>一、皇城门旧止系建康府门，增盖屋九间，其下仍旧两门，亦不曾增设两观，盖非古制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216676_comment'></div>今相度旧门东西两傍以仗舍地作为两观，于见两门之中别开一正门，列为三门，地步可以安排有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216676_comment'></div>却移拆旧门屋，别立两观，就上建立屋宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216676_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1216676'>一、古礼，天子有三朝，外朝以询万民，内朝日见群臣，燕朝日退而听政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216676_comment'></div>本朝大庆殿即古之外朝，故正旦大朝会与明堂行礼等皆御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216676_comment'></div>文德殿即古之内朝，故月朔过殿与行册礼等皆御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216676_comment'></div>紫宸、垂拱殿即古之燕朝，故月望不过殿，唤仗入閤，与六参官、番客辞见等，皆御紫宸，日朝见常参官皆御垂拱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216676_comment'></div>此皆不可阙者，惟集英、皇仪两殿可减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216676_comment'></div>令旧止有朝殿一所，应明堂、朝会并朔望日朝之礼并行于一殿之上，恐非古制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216676_comment'></div>今相度，若以朝殿西取直平分为外庭一排，盖垂拱殿，即其前可盖文德殿，却移朝殿向前为大庆殿，以旧基盖紫宸殿，其馀西面盖两省、枢密院等，则与《周官》及汴京制度略同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216676_comment'></div>其侵入禁中隙地五十馀丈，若不侵入，不唯别无地段□宫殿亦不可设于他所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216676_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1216676'>一、汴京左右掖、东华门入内直至紫宸、垂拱殿前，通行过路各有别门，如左右升龙、承天、银台、嘉肃、宣祐、謻门等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216676_comment'></div>其与禁中内外分隔处，非有殿宇，即是重廊，所以察奸防微，以示深密尊严之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216676_comment'></div>今行宫止朝殿前有行宫门两重外，其馀并无别门，其禁中分隔处多是筑墙为限，恐非旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216676_comment'></div>今相度，若许依仿前项措置，即朝殿西有紫宸殿，小殿东有廊，其所经由过路，并可量要会去处各立别门，并分设班房，以居卫士，实为经久之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216676_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1216676'>一、中书、门下两省并两后省、枢密院、学士院职事皆在禁庭，汴京皆设于文德殿之西东，于文德殿两间为隔门过道，从官、常朝官下马，宰执则由右掖门直趋紫宸主廊下马，以为等杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216676_comment'></div>今两省、枢密院并在外，与尚书省同为一处，入朝下马并在行宫门，恐非旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216676_comment'></div>今相度，若紫宸、垂拱殿南许依前项措置，即其西剩地，两省、枢密、学士院可略依汴京盖造，并宰执、常参、六参官下马处，亦依得汴京旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216676_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1216676'>一、今来相度殿宇及两廊屋，并是据旧地步打量丈尺间架安排，若蒙施行，即其屋间架高阔深浅若合依仿旧制，难以别更增展，内文德、紫宸、垂拱殿恐地步或窄，即合随宜减退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216676_comment'></div>别具申明，乞修内司参定制度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216676_comment'></div>右具如前<span class='inlineComment2'>（《石林奏议》卷一○。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216676_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1216676'>「别」、「立」、「观」三字原残，据汲古阁本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1216676_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年5月</a>　在建康任。五月十三日，金人败盟，分四道侵宋。二十日前后，石林有《闻边报示诸将》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻边报示诸将</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526659")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526659'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526659'>插羽惊传赤白囊，胡行如鬼尚跳梁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526659'>颇闻庙算无遗策，但遣封人谨豫防。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526659'>送死定知天悔祸，追奔宁使汝争彊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526659'>将军剩有封侯印，尽扫无令一镞亡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526659'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526659_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年5月</a>　在建康任，五月二十日前后，有奏札。作品：《奏金贼败盟乞下三大将措置捍御札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏乞下刘錡李世辅进兵讨贼札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216604' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216604' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216604?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏金贼败盟乞下三大将措置捍御劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216604")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216604_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216604'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216604'>臣今月二十一日，准寿春府探报，虏骑侵犯东京，打虏已至拱州、应天府，未明虚实，寻已两具奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216604_comment'></div>顷睹淮西宣抚司探报，与臣一同，并有录白到伪榜，必亦具奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216604_comment'></div>臣窃惟虏情变诈不测，盖有自来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216604_comment'></div>昨张通古来使之后，虽归我旧疆，朝廷寻遣王伦等报聘，既留王伦不遣，莫将继行，又不即迎，旷日持久，包藏祸心，人固疑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216604_comment'></div>今果猖蹶，乃以盛夏弓解马疲之时，遽至王畿，其志必是秋冬欲如往年深入，观我所为，徐为进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216604_comment'></div>故先入京师，休养士马，复占昨来留下米斛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216604_comment'></div>仍因二麦成熟，苛敛拘收，积聚粮食，至秋深长驱南下，为必冲突之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216604_comment'></div>若我有以御之，则因所积之粮，且坚壁相持，万一我有间隙可乘，则鼓行而前，惟所欲为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216604_comment'></div>陛下圣谋宏远，慎终图始，必皆素有定议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216604_comment'></div>臣备员疆吏，职思其忧，不敢不为过计妄意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216604_comment'></div>议者或谓虏势频年衰弱，去夏腹心自相诛戮，惧为我所窥，故特为此谋以自抗，暂至京师，未必更能前进，我不可为之震扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216604_comment'></div>或以为莫将奉使未回，虏欲取我岁币，贪婪不赀，及邀求礼数，狂悖非分，以我未即顺从，故以重兵压境劫胁，以幸得志，我始疑之，不可使与争锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216604_comment'></div>若果出此，则固无足虑，我但持重，胜之以理可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216604_comment'></div>如其不然，出我所料之外，一旦横行，而我无预备，则事至岂可旋为之谋哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216604_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216604_comment'></div>虏素有易我之心，谓其衰弱，则非臣所得知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216604_comment'></div>若邀求狂悖，则前已见于事矣，安能保其必止于东京？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216604_comment'></div>盖虏之南侵者凡再，建炎三年陛下巡海上，杜充迎降，诸将败，十万人望风溃散，故乘势得以入浙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216604_comment'></div>其易我者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216604_comment'></div>绍兴五年，以刘豫为乡导，再复大入，陛下进临平江，诸将并会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216604_comment'></div>虽杨沂中迎敌，一战破之，然不能继为图，使师老从容得去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216604_comment'></div>其易我者二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216604_comment'></div>今不稍更前辙，赫示王威，督责中外，日夜并手共为，及至秋冬，尚恐不及，若更少缓，便得料我但如平日，其气愈盛，其锋愈锐，则何所不可肆哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216604_comment'></div>臣闻上兵伐谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216604_comment'></div>臣不知虏欲复旧疆，朝廷姑且听之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216604_comment'></div>欲坚守以俟，则中原兵力寡弱，城池器械皆未尝料理，未可遽与之较。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216604_comment'></div>若姑且听之，则莫若先伐其谋，亟下中原诸州，乘其兵未集，尽将见管米斛并民间二麦特为措置，或令般运，或令焚弃，勿为彼有，纵有不及，胜于不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216604_comment'></div>彼所恃者先已失图，我却部分诸将掎角连衡，分据要地，示以欲战之形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216604_comment'></div>姑以和议应之，佯为小屈，使彼曲我直，而内实严为守备，纤悉周尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216604_comment'></div>今诸将兵训练日久，各精熟，畜锐思奋，人怀踊跃，闻虏亦自知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216604_comment'></div>张皇六师，亦先王用兵之术所不能免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216604_comment'></div>如虏纵未即知畏，岂不内怀疑阻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216604_comment'></div>我益商度军食，分置沿流诸郡，我之所积者日广，彼之所仰者日耗，进不得前，退不得守，虽欲久留，势有不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216604_comment'></div>而后我或欲优柔涵容，尚存和议，以奉迎太母；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216604_comment'></div>欲乘其弊，定与决战，使彼惧而归我太母，苟出于一，无不可行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1216604_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐睿察，参酌累年方略，反覆熟议，无使我在其术内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1216604_comment'></div>古者师克在和不在众，虽有良将，苟非同心，未易成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1216604_comment'></div>汉陈平号智略无遗，方诸吕为变，周勃以太尉握重兵，犹无以为策，得陆贾之言，奉金交欢，始能坐胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1216604_comment'></div>唐以九节度兵围史思明于相州，李光弼、郭子仪在其间，而计虑不同，人各自异，卒为思明所败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1216604_comment'></div>今大兵所恃，惟韩世忠、张俊、岳飞三将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1216604_comment'></div>臣欲乞朝廷先定大计，更命三将各具所见，如何则守，如何则战，守以何道，战以何术，孰当锋居前，孰勒兵殿后，如何以为声援，如何以为策应，一二条上，取所可行者就以付之，各尽其谋，更相究知，以责功效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1216604_comment'></div>仍下诏慰勉，俾务辑睦，苟无同异，躬率部曲，一以社稷为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1216604_comment'></div>古之言兵者以谓如常山之蛇，击其首则尾应，击其尾则首应，而艰难相济，譬之同舟遇风，虽胡越且无异心，况位兼将相，比肩并立者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1216604_comment'></div>此武王有臣三千，人同一心，所以胜纣之亿万人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1216604_comment'></div>臣智识浅陋，不明远略，滥守陪都，外固边圉，敢不竭尽忠款，少效区区之愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1216604_comment'></div>冒渎天威，臣无任惶惧陨越之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1216604_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1216604_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞下刘锜李世辅进兵讨贼劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216605")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216605'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216605'>臣近以虏骑侵犯河南，二十四日尝具管见奏陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216605_comment'></div>伏睹手诏，显暴虏渝盟失信之罪，困虐中原无已之恶，一伸王威，宣达众愤，中外呼舞，远近同辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216605_comment'></div>相继大号起刘光世招抚三京，以坏散贼谋，携贰其党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216605_comment'></div>刘锜复立功顺昌，军声士气，鼓勇百倍，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216605_comment'></div>臣滥守陪都，外当一面，主忧臣辱，不敢不尽死节，少佐旰食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216605_comment'></div>数日来，博采人情，以听舆论，皆以虏诡诈凭陵，人人怀怒蓄锐，有北向殄灭之意，与前数岁不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216605_comment'></div>此乃天启中兴，虏恶贯盈，自取覆亡之日，非人力所能为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216605_comment'></div>锜既首挫其锋，其兆已见，议者皆谓锜孤军远立，将士用命，所以能先诸将立功，须朝廷极力主张激励，使得尽其心，不惟可令虏望风沮屈，国势当亦自此遂振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216605_comment'></div>窃闻朝廷已遣李世辅、王德往应援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216605_comment'></div>世辅虏所深怨，如其用李成、郦琼等，诚为得策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216605_comment'></div>兼其人骁勇沉厚，深达敌情，侪类多所推称，以为朝廷用之得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216605_comment'></div>但颇愿多与之兵，略与锜相当，使与锜更为形势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216605_comment'></div>锜驻顺昌，世辅驻泗州，夹淮东西，掎角相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216605_comment'></div>更敕韩世忠、张俊各以精骑巡所部境上，以为之殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216605_comment'></div>王德一军，往来游击于锜、世辅之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216605_comment'></div>虏近所下诸郡，皆不过百馀骑，传檄得其降书即去，百姓向背，无所与责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216605_comment'></div>如景详、王彦充辈，前此本非归我，皆虏留为腹心，潜相窥觇者，故闻变尽甘心虏命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216605_comment'></div>其所守既无备，王德可以坐擒，虏固不能发兵往救，又不能分兵并守，则故疆自已收复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216605_comment'></div>我擒其守长，厚抚其民，亦可就食粮斛，绝其后计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216605_comment'></div>虏所保者，惟在京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216605_comment'></div>据探报，虏兵至京师者不满三万人，非叛兵即签军，正兵无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1216605_comment'></div>若锜、世辅斥堠明远，伺得其便，即命鼓行而前，世忠后继之，直薄城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1216605_comment'></div>自不妨刘光世一面招抚，凶悍者诛灭，柔顺者归附，虏无所恃，必惧而遁去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1216605_comment'></div>若闭城固守，旋追兵国中，当此时暑，疾驱远来，人疲马困，我迎击河上，可以必得，虏乃在吾腹中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1216605_comment'></div>此万世一时，不可失之机会也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1216605_comment'></div>少有稽缓，使虏得整兵而来，或刘锜力不能持，退舍则虏复得志，计将难谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1216605_comment'></div>臣衰懦不武，素不闲习军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1216605_comment'></div>历考载籍，自古用兵，凡大胜败，未有不因士气所向；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1216605_comment'></div>士气所向，未有不顺人心所欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1216605_comment'></div>臣前所论奏，以虏犯境之初，未见其兵厚薄，我未整饬军伍，故且乞夺其储积，无守旧辙，矫前日畏避之过，张皇六师，过为堤备，以待其衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1216605_comment'></div>今虏形已见，正乘机定计之时，此之所陈，盖得于人心同欲，非臣狂妄之私，不敢隐默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1216605_comment'></div>伏望圣慈更命大臣参考熟议，少留圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1216605_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1216605_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1216605_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1216605'>〔贴黄〕臣伏闻异时大将多患持重顾望，不即击贼，至遣大臣督战，犹怀前却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1216605_comment'></div>今刘锜、李世辅先立功于前，则拥重兵于后者亦自不能已，必须悉力争奋，尤于朝廷驾驭之权深为得体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1216605_comment'></div>伏乞睿察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1216605_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1216605'>〔又贴黄〕臣据今日探报，河南孙晖亦已却敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1216605_comment'></div>虏宿州等处所留兵尽已起发前往滑州、徐州，不知何意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1216605_comment'></div>伺间捣虚，尤不可缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1216605_comment'></div>伏乞睿察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1216605_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年5月</a>　在建康任，五月二十五日前后，有《敌兵复过河王师出讨》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526660' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526660' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526660?labeling=true' target='_blank'>虏酋复过河王师出讨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526660")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526660_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526660'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526660'>羽檄初徵天下兵，误惭一阵守王城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526660'>秦兵出项<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作岭）</span>终何得，汉将征辽会扫平。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526660'>便遣幽燕驱号令，久怜河洛污膻腥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526660'>书生岂解论几事，讵信平凉有劫盟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526660'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526660'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_526660_0'>⑴ 自注：始议请（影宋本、四库本作讲）和，余数言其不然。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526660_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年5月</a>　在建康任，五月底，有贺启。作品：《贺三京招抚刘太保启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216705?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺三京招抚刘太保启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216705")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216705_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216705'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216705'>方叔壮猷，夙任兴周之寄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216705_comment'></div>召公为保，载勤分陕之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216705_comment'></div>孚号载飏，裔夷震叠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216705_comment'></div>伏惟某官忠诚许国，术略佐时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216705_comment'></div>总御六师，早席将门之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216705_comment'></div>廓清四海，屡扶王室之危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216705_comment'></div>憬彼犬戎，复干虎旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216705_comment'></div>虽王赫斯怒，所歼者渠魁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216705_comment'></div>而民怀有仁，愿适者乐土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216705_comment'></div>况仇葛来苏之望，皆灵台乐德之人，不待招携，咸知效顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216705_comment'></div>倒戈内附，岂惟见于前徒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216705_comment'></div>免胄纵观，孰不归于吾父？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216705_comment'></div>一蒙开纳，尽洗腥膻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216705_comment'></div>某久幸从游，欣闻播告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216705_comment'></div>莫遂瞻承之志，徒深庆抃之诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1216705_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年5月</a>　在建康任，五月底，遣晁公昂往长江边巡视营垒工事，有诗。作品：《遣晁公昂按行濒江营垒》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526661' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526661' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526661?labeling=true' target='_blank'>遣晁公昂按行濒江营垒</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526661")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526661_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526661'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526661'>他日传烽望夕烟，重来老更负戎旃。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526661'>我言固自平平耳，王事那辞数数然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526661'>转饷未应劳木马，摧锋犹或要戈船。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526661'>天威本自无多杀，万一征和属此年<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：时闻虏遣乌陵思谟来请和。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526661'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526661_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2fd899664d94428189e3342095d494c5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2fd899664d94428189e3342095d494c5");'><span id='2fd899664d94428189e3342095d494c5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1141')">1140-1141年</a>，64-65岁</div><div id='2fd899664d94428189e3342095d494c5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　冬，在建康，有《登南城》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登南城</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526663")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526663'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526663'>大江南渡是长干，北望清淮岁已寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526663'>废垒至今闻鹤唳，苍山从古自龙蟠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526663'>鬓毛白尽空看镜，髀肉销来尚据鞍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526663'>折箠不能笞黠虏，遗民<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>犹有汉衣冠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526663'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526663'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_526663_0'>⑴ 原缺，据影宋本补，四库本作规</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526663_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月4日</a>　在建康府任，二月初四，金兵再度侵淮西，石林劝请大将张俊速出兵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月6日</a>　在建康府任，二月六日，有感怀诗。作品：《二月六日敌兵犯历阳方出师客自吴江来有寄声道湖山之适趣其归者慨然写怀》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二月六日虏兵犯历阳方出师客自吴江来有寄声道湖山之适趣其归者慨然写怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年2月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526673")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526673'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526673'>松江浪静如镜平，菰蒲长春秋水生。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526673'>晴沙回雁久未到，坐想白鸥增眼明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526673'>五年辜负钓船约，故人疑我真逃盟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526673'>岂知尘缨不易濯，正想沧浪之水清。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526673'>朝来铁马暗江北，中流叠鼓云涛倾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526673'>楼船十万下采石，旗纛灭没天戈横。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526673'>书生事业今乃尔，授钺孰敢辞专征。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526673'>岂无传檄走飞骑，漫复长啸登高城。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526673'>文思天子民父母，大度未忍鏖奇兵。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526673'>澶渊一矢安五世，明日傥或传诸营。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526673'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_526673_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月</a>　在建康府任。二月十八日，柘皋大捷。稍后，石林有诗二首。作品：《淮西军连日告捷喜成口号二首》其一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《淮西军连日告捷喜成口号二首》其二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淮西军大破贼兵连六告捷喜成口号二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526674'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526674'>一战聊麾十万师，西来捷报走黄旗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526674'>六骡壮骑终须<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作影宋本作亡）</span>去，九虎将军亦谩为<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526674'>面内疲民元不改<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，从中胜算自无遗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526674'>临轩想见天颜喜，百辟欢声动玉墀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526674'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526674'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_526674_0'>⑴ 自注：贼（四库本作敌）将龙虎、辅国等将军，皆其用事酋。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_526674_0'>⑵ 自注：柘皋之捷，驱虏吾民尽复得之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_526674_0'>⑶ 自注：自贼（四库本作敌）兵过淮，凡指授诸将尽从中出。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526674_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_526675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_526675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526675'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526675'>蛇豕何知阚近坰，且欣鏖战扫膻腥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526675'>寄声急走破羌帖，归路还经征虏亭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526675'>多难兵间头更白<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：事见光武。）</span>，放怀物外眼终青。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526675'>花残不负岩边约，更看前焚老上庭<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：老上龙庭，匈奴地名。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_1216708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺张少师奏捷启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1216708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216708'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216708'>出将王命，前讨邦仇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216708_comment'></div>万里犬羊，既望风而知畏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216708_comment'></div>六师貔虎，咸奋义而争趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216708_comment'></div>果扫妖氛，共成大烈，伏惟欢庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216708_comment'></div>恭以某官勋高宗社，名重华夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216708_comment'></div>被公衮以临戎，孰出三司之右；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216708_comment'></div>总将坛而申令，更隆百胜之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216708_comment'></div>耸中外之欣欢，雪神人之深愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216708_comment'></div>某获联疆事，首奉捷音，欢抃之私，敷宣罔既。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1216708_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月</a>　在建康府任，二月二十三日前后，有《小饮示幕府》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>小饮示幕府</a><span
