"poem_title_526678")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526678'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526678'>边书日夜急，王旅方徂征。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526678'>我非刘越石，长啸徒登城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526678'>缅想豺与虎，行当筑鲵鲸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526678'>传车日边来，风雷走天声<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526678'>黄旗三面至，捷奏纷纷横。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526678'>天险<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作堑）</span>限南北，长江正东倾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526678'>诸君亦良苦，唾口<span class='inlineComment2'>（影宋本作手）</span>争请缨。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526678'>谁云凌烟阁，自昔无书生。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526678'>卮酒安足辞，勉当建雄名<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526678'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_526678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526678'><span class='label'>按：</span>以上《石林居士建康集》卷一<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_526678_0'>⑴ 自注：连日中遣主（四库本作奄、影宋本作王）人赍金帛犒师者经过。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_8_526678_0'>⑵ 自注：李贺诗请君试上凌烟阁，若个书生万户侯。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526678_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月27日</a>　在建康府任，二月二十七，上奏称贺淮西军败敌。石林以馈饷诸军有劳，朝廷益嘉之。作品：《奏淮西宣抚使杀败金人札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏淮西宣抚使杀败金人劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年2月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216501")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216501'>臣窃惟黠虏去岁败盟，盗据京师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216501_comment'></div>今年狂突，径至淮甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216501_comment'></div>驱集丑类，竭国远来，睥睨江壖，无所畏惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216501_comment'></div>陛下圣文神武，逆折凶威，申命将臣，授之成算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216501_comment'></div>曾不踰旬，以十五万之众计穷力屈，全师鏖战，连告六捷，败亡丧衄，狼狈走遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216501_comment'></div>名王贵酋奔踣于道，壮士健马物故相乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216501_comment'></div>自用兵以来，未有此举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216501_comment'></div>伸人神之宿愤，雪宗庙之深雠，鼓舞欢呼，中外一口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216501_comment'></div>自此擒馘凶渠，廓清畿甸，尽还故土，克复中原，近在旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216501_comment'></div>臣误蒙寄委，实当控扼，不能身先士卒，少效微劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216501_comment'></div>疆事有守，无缘躬诣冕旒，少伸庆贺之诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1216501_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年2月</a>　在建康府任，二月，石林闻嘉奖之诏，上谢表。作品：《谢奏陈金师退败降诏奖谕表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216487' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216487' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216487?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢奏陈金贼退败降诏奖谕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216487")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216487_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216487'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216487'>正王者之兵，既张天讨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216487_comment'></div>申舆人之诵，少达下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216487_comment'></div>仰荷眷慈，特膺殊奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216487_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣少而不武，老益无能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216487_comment'></div>当长江御侮之冲，适丑虏败盟之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216487_comment'></div>惟纣臣有亿万众，皆倒戈攻后之徒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216487_comment'></div>而楚恶已数十年，亦曷丧偕亡之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216487_comment'></div>戎马既驾，我武惟扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216487_comment'></div>敌所忾以争先，首摧凶焰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216487_comment'></div>取彼残而共殄，卒扫妖氛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216487_comment'></div>惭无矢石之勤，滥窃玺书之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216487_comment'></div>敢怀掠美，辄奏罔功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216487_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下谋发自中，威行无外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216487_comment'></div>不震不动，图回每尽于敌情；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216487_comment'></div>能弱能强，终始弗逃于圣算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216487_comment'></div>欲励服劳之士，故捐假宠之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216487_comment'></div>臣力以病衰，恳祈退免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216487_comment'></div>尧言争诵，虽莫酬君父不赀之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216487_comment'></div>汉札细书，犹足示子孙无穷之宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216487_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1216487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1216487'><span class='label'>按：</span>《石林居士建康集》卷五。又见《景定建康志》卷三六，清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷三七。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1216487_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年3月</a>　在建康府任，三月十六日后，刻石记淮西大捷。作品：《书为山亭石上》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216766' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216766' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216766?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书为山亭石上</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216766")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216766_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216766'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216766'>绍兴辛酉正月，兀术以众二十万入寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216766_comment'></div>壬戌，渡淮据合淝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216766_comment'></div>二月辛未，淮西宣抚使军出征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216766_comment'></div>癸酉，渡江，是夕，败贼前锋，壁历阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216766_comment'></div>丙子，又败之于含山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216766_comment'></div>戊寅，又败之于巢县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216766_comment'></div>己卯，又败之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216766_comment'></div>辛巳，复寇和州，又败之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216766_comment'></div>壬午，又败之于全椒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216766_comment'></div>癸未、甲申，又连败之于关口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216766_comment'></div>丙戌，又败之于仙宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216766_comment'></div>丁亥，又败之于柘皋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216766_comment'></div>己丑，遂败兀术于店步，复合淝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216766_comment'></div>庚寅，王师入庐州，贼尽过淮奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216766_comment'></div>乙未，班师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216766_comment'></div>丁卯，献俘于王所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216766_comment'></div>江南东路安抚制置大使叶某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1216766_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年3月</a>　在建康府任，三月，上《第三次乞宫观第一状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>第三次乞宫观第一状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216520")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216520'>右，臣去年春，尝以疾病，三具奏乞罢免府事，退领闲秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216520_comment'></div>伏蒙圣恩，降诏书不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216520_comment'></div>继以专委营缮行宫事，不敢固守愚诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216520_comment'></div>方俟伻图措画略定，再伸前请，复遇疆事遽兴，濒江正当捍御，义难顾身，因遂勉强，迁延至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216520_comment'></div>伏念臣衰瘁馀生，筋力愈惫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216520_comment'></div>留都重地，在今日正须得人，而叨冒养疴，首尾已及三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216520_comment'></div>虽夙夜不敢少懈，讫无秋毫补报，罪戾之积，固不待言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216520_comment'></div>兹者幸遇天威既伸，狂虏知畏，去冬以来，戢兵远遁，边境少安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216520_comment'></div>今者将及解严，于臣私义，可以自列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216520_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐矜怜，检会臣前后奏章，特除一在外宫观差遣，任便居住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216520_comment'></div>负恩而去，虽无以仰酬覆帱之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216520_comment'></div>陈力不能，亦庶几粗免颠越之惧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1216520_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年4月</a>　在建康府任，四月，上乞宫观《第二状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　是年，在建康府任，有祈雨文。作品：《诸庙祈雨文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年6月</a>　在建康府任，六月初，上乞宫观《第三状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年6月16日</a>　在建康府任，六月十六日，升观文殿学士，续任江东安抚置制大使兼知建康府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年6月</a>　在建康府任，六月，有辞免观文殿学士再任奏状。作品：《辞免观文殿学士再任状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216523' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216523' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216523?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免观文殿学士再任状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216523")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216523_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216523'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216523'>右，臣今月某日，准御前金字牌降到尚书省劄子一道，伏奉圣旨，除臣观文殿学士，令再任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216523_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知攸措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216523_comment'></div>伏念臣衰病馀生，昨者误蒙圣知，起之闲废，付以一面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216523_comment'></div>虽夙夜罄竭疲驽，自知无以报称，故频年屡干天听，乞从罢免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216523_comment'></div>仰荷眷私，未即报可，迁延已及终更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216523_comment'></div>方跼蹐以俟俞旨，忽闻有此除授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216523_comment'></div>退量已试之效，实无秋毫小补，岂敢重愧军民，辄怀贪冒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216523_comment'></div>兼观文殿学士职名，祖宗故事，藩镇外除无几，臣独何人，可当异数？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216523_comment'></div>伏望天高听卑，俯察危恳，特赐寝罢新命，检会臣前后累奏，除一外任宫观差遣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1216523_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年6月</a>　在建康府任，六月，有辞免观文殿学士札子。作品：《辞免观文殿学士札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216503?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免观文殿学士劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216503")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216503_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216503'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216503'>臣近者蒙恩除观文殿学士，令再任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216503_comment'></div>寻以超躐过分，具奏辞免，愿请闲秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216503_comment'></div>伏奉诏书，未赐俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216503_comment'></div>一介贱微，仰干天造，逡巡留令，罪不容诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216503_comment'></div>所有再任职事，臣不敢叠有烦喋，候降到告，即恭禀圣训，依旧交管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216503_comment'></div>别具表称谢外，窃惟观文殿职名，祖宗创置甚重，近岁非自知枢密院以上善罢，未尝轻除；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216503_comment'></div>其馀必藩邸旧恩，寅缘攀附，边防剧任，开拓封疆，仅乃得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216503_comment'></div>至于常侍帷幄，外守方镇，累更出入，时示褒崇者，不过数人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216503_comment'></div>而臣自省，皆无一得，徒以待罪岁久，遽先近服，稽之公论，岂曰宜然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216503_comment'></div>况臣去秋已荷洪私，加进资政殿大学士，于今未及一年，尤难侥冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216503_comment'></div>夙夕震惧，无以苟安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216503_comment'></div>非常之恩，既已仰承于异眷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216503_comment'></div>量己之戒，尚冀少尽于愚衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216503_comment'></div>敢望矜从，终赐寝罢，庶几尚可勉殚馀力，未至遽速烦言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1216503_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年6月</a>　在建康府任，六月，有谢观文殿学士表。作品：《谢观文殿学士表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢观文殿学士表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216492")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216492_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216492'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216492'>恩非所称，难逃负乘之讥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216492_comment'></div>命出非常，莫获循墙之避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216492_comment'></div>重勤训饬，倍极兢危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216492_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃惟学士建名，虽兴前代；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216492_comment'></div>近臣分职，盖始本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216492_comment'></div>至于易文明顾问之称，冠秘殿宠褒之盛，仰观故事，尤号殊荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216492_comment'></div>爰历艰难，盖多勋德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216492_comment'></div>以旧臣宣劳于外，固不乏人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216492_comment'></div>由建炎越次而除，则无前比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216492_comment'></div>乃如固陋，其敢叨逾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216492_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下义笃臣邻，忧深中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216492_comment'></div>谓与之名者将求其实，而使之礼者必报其忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216492_comment'></div>故于贤贤蒐选之间，每有下下并包之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216492_comment'></div>重念臣受材至薄，涉世多艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216492_comment'></div>少日量能，尚有满盈之戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216492_comment'></div>暮年多取，岂无颠覆之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216492_comment'></div>虽倾竭于馀生，恐终辜于大造。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1216492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1216492'><span class='label'>按：</span>《石林居士建康集》卷五。又见《景定建康志》卷三六，清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷一九。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1216492_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年6月</a>　在建康府任，六月，有谢表。作品：《谢再任表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢再任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216491")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216491'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216491'>三载黜幽，方惧干于明宪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216491_comment'></div>再命而伛，忽荐被于异恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216491_comment'></div>不称所蒙，重惭非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216491_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣早由疏贱，误窃宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216491_comment'></div>先朝滥寘于从班，本无报效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216491_comment'></div>陛下擢登于政路，已迫衰残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216491_comment'></div>自知陈力之无堪，唯有乞身而退屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216491_comment'></div>逮谋帅阃，仍玷留都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216491_comment'></div>故连年虽幸于苟安，而无岁不祈于罢免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216491_comment'></div>仰蒙全贷，偶及终更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216491_comment'></div>惟鼯鼠五技之既穷，亦驽马十驾之何及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216491_comment'></div>岂期过听，更责后图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216491_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下体貌群工，作兴庶政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216491_comment'></div>念其拳拳忠款，初非有爱于馀生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216491_comment'></div>察其龊龊廉勤，犹未遽罹于大过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216491_comment'></div>姑令代匮，岂曰因能？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216491_comment'></div>丁宁殆至于再三，感励难酬于万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216491_comment'></div>臣敢不钦承德意，勉激愚衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216491_comment'></div>苟子产见推，晚或容于郑俗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1216491_comment'></div>虽廉颇已老，终无憾于赵人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1216491_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1216491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1216491'><span class='label'>按：</span>《石林居士建康集》卷五。又见《景定建康志》卷三六，清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷三一。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1216491_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年6月</a>　在建康府任，六月，有谢启。作品：《除观文殿学士再任谢执政启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216709' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216709' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216709?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除观文殿学士再任谢执政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216709")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216709_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216709'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216709'>及瓜而代，初无可录之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216709_comment'></div>采菲不遗，遽窃非常之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216709_comment'></div>祗承眷渥，莫获牢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216709_comment'></div>伏念某本乏异能，过叨重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216709_comment'></div>空疏之学，固斐然不知裁之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216709_comment'></div>戆拙之材，况老矣无能为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216709_comment'></div>故承乏因循者三岁，而乞身恳请者六章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216709_comment'></div>何期避剧以求閒，更复逾涯而拜赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216709_comment'></div>岂无再割，人共笑其铅刀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216709_comment'></div>虽已强陈，己亦惭其刍狗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216709_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官权衡庶物，柱石本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216709_comment'></div>追叙禹谟，协九功而共治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216709_comment'></div>辅成周命，倡十乱以同心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216709_comment'></div>未遑舍旧以图新，姑亦绝长而补短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216709_comment'></div>安国无功自愧，本幸罢归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216709_comment'></div>颍川有诏如前，何能愈治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216709_comment'></div>未知报塞，徒有铭藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216709_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1216709_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_4_526698_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年9月19日</a>　在建康府任。九月十九日，府前居民失火，石林奋力出救。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年9月</a>　在建康府任，九月十九日后，有为火灾待罪二札子。作品：《奏居民遗火待罪札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《再奏居民遗火待罪札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216505' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216505' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216505?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再奏居民遗火待罪劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216505")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216505_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216505'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216505'>臣近缘本府居民遗漏，延及州治，具奏自劾待罪，乞行降黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216505_comment'></div>寻再具劄子，陈布犬马之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216505_comment'></div>近准尚书省劄子，九月二十五日奉圣旨，留司委寄甚重，令某安职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216505_comment'></div>孤蹇馀生，仰戴天地覆载之慈，跼蹐无所自容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216505_comment'></div>缘臣不职之罪，终不敢苟逃，伏望圣慈特赐检会施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1216505_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年9月</a>　在建康府任，九月二十五日，上赦遗火罪。稍后，石林有谢表。作品：《谢居民遗火待罪安职表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《谢军寨遗火赦罪表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216493' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216493' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216493?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢居民遗火待罪令安置表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216493")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216493_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216493'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216493'>无功受禄，已愧素餐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216493_comment'></div>有罪不诛，复叨宽典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216493_comment'></div>仰惟大施，毕出至仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216493_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣误以疲驽，荐蒙委寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216493_comment'></div>方戎马戒严之际，且旱旸害稼之馀，反侧未安，凋残易困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216493_comment'></div>虽无挠狱市，每师齐相静治之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216493_comment'></div>而慎守封疆，敢忘鲁人请事之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216493_comment'></div>讫无寸效，重愧本心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216493_comment'></div>可容非意之忧，更速旷官之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216493_comment'></div>法当显黜，恩独原情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216493_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下德极含洪，道全忠恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216493_comment'></div>八柄并用，固将昭示于赏刑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216493_comment'></div>三宥所加，终欲掩藏其过失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216493_comment'></div>幸其可再，居不遑宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216493_comment'></div>臣敢不上体眷慈，勉扶衰病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216493_comment'></div>遵简书而奔命，未敢言归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216493_comment'></div>记焚室以宽征，庶无失所。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1216493_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1216493'><span class='label'>按：</span>《石林居士建康集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷三八。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1216493_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1216488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216488' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216488?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢军寨遗火放罪表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216488")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216488_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216488'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216488'>奉职不虔，自贻旷败；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216488_comment'></div>抚躬引咎，方俟谴诃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216488_comment'></div>仰荷宽慈，曲从贷释<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216488_comment'></div>伏念臣素无远用，本实凡材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216488_comment'></div>沉迷簿领之间，徒劳无补；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216488_comment'></div>出入兵戈之际，愈久益疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216488_comment'></div>误窃守符，仍司留钥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216488_comment'></div>既不能折冲强敌，少尽力于疆陲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216488_comment'></div>又无以和辑疲民，使安生于闾里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216488_comment'></div>致令非意，罔戒不虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216488_comment'></div>知重废于官常，敢幸逃于吏议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216488_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下慎微接下，以德行仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216488_comment'></div>虽爱悯黎元，如御朽索之马；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216488_comment'></div>而保全臣子，每漏吞舟之鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216488_comment'></div>念将迫于终更，俾不污于后累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216488_comment'></div>臣敢不勉殚衰懦，深务省循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216488_comment'></div>岂不怀归，未遂乞身之请；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216488_comment'></div>退思补过，终惭报国之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216488_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1216488_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1216488'><span id='poem_sentence_12_526715'>回风送远响，墟里生晚烟。<div id='poem_sentence_12_526715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_526715'>吾庐怅何许，东望良慨然。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　在建康府任，初夏，同徐度复游石头城清凉寺，有诗。作品：《明日复游石头城清凉寺再用前韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526716' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_5_526716'>颓檐<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作颜）</span>翳崖壁，过午不得旋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526716_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526716'>像佛<span id='poem_sentence_6_526719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526719'>坐怀北山岩，未见西溪涟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年6月</a>　在建康府任，六月，乞宫观未允，再上乞宫观札子。作品：《再乞宫观札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216507?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再乞宫观劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216507")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216507'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216507'>臣近尝陈乞在外宫观一任，今月十二日准都进奏院递到诏书一道，伏蒙圣恩，过加温言，曲垂镌谕，未赐俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216507_comment'></div>天地之造，出于生成，在臣犬马之分，岂所宜得？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216507_comment'></div>威惧战悚，无地自容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216507_comment'></div>重念臣昨者自弃山林，误荷收录，置之方面，固当竭尽死节，以图报效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216507_comment'></div>而臣每不安位，屡祈退屏，实以德薄器浅，难堪重寄，年龄晚暮，义合知止，所以不避斧钺之诛，叠干渊听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216507_comment'></div>今兹迁延再任，又已踰年，疆事既宁，人皆安业，坐尸厚禄，尤愧本心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216507_comment'></div>外怀叨窃无补之忧，内迫亢满疾颠之畏，此臣朝夕所以不遑宁处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216507_comment'></div>伏望圣慈俯加矜悯，傥获始终大赐，特全造物之私，庶几黾勉馀年，粗守保身之戒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1216507_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年6月</a>　在建康府任，六月，有次韵马参谋诗。作品：《次韵马参谋新作山亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526729' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526729' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526729?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵马参谋新作山亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_526729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526729'>苦厌簿书迷老景，坐怀丘壑寄颓龄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年6月</a>　在建康府任，六月，有诗与方参议唱和。作品：《方参议用前韵记尝过余石林次韵答之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526730' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526730' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526730?labeling=true' target='_blank'>方参议用前韵记尝过余石林次韵答之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526730")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_526730_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526730'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526730'>不复襄阳写孟亭，草斋人道是丹青。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526730'>那知客自从文举，但怪山能养伯龄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526730'>世味无多真潦倒，归心欲寄每丁宁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526730'>遥闻径竹添新影，更想岩花作远馨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526730'>夜鹤未应真怨别，江鸥须信久忘形。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526730'>地偏故逐渊明远，风好常随御寇泠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526730'>痴坐正怜尘满案，醉眠终倚石为屏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526730'>瀛洲学士烦追赋，尚记沧波接洞庭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526730'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_526730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526730'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_526730_0'>⑴ 自注：卞山后即太湖，正与洞庭东西两山相望。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526730_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　在建康府任，夏，有诗次韵马参谋。作品：《次韵马参谋蒋山开堂饭素》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526726' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_526726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526726'>相追更喜同枝<span class='inlineComment2'>（影宋本作扶）</span>策，得意遥知了斲轮。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526726_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　在建康府任，夏，有诗。作品：《诸幕府见和复答二首》其一。<span "poem_title_526721")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526721_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526721'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526721'>他年落笔坐生风，下舍诸郎敢长雄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526721'>操缦不能陪众手，斲轮终自付良工。<div ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526722")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_526722_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526722'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526722'>戏弄扁舟泊宅村，却寻三径筑茅墩。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526722'>云边此意真谁解，剩作新诗与细论。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526722'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_526722_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526723' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526723' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526723?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_526723_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526723'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526723'>水槛新开似浣花，傍溪须更作浮槎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526723'>祗应屡费王弘酒，时要清樽对落霞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526723'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_526723_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526724' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526724' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526724?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526724'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526724'>不惜囊钱信手空，荒田却拟望年丰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526724'>天公可是怜风月，判遣诗人一例穷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526724'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_526724_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526725' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526725' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526725?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_526725_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526725'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526725'>卢橘杨梅已及时，我归先自在前期。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526725'>平生不作宣明面，浪愧将军建鼓旗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526725'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_526725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526725'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_526725_0'>⑴ 仁声旧居城东泊宅村，张志和常所游也。今徙西溪，作云茅庵，因东岗为小亭，号茅墩。欲傍溪开水槛，久无资。会郡守有馈之酒五十壶，不敢饮，亟易之，乃克成。有田数十亩，常苦下潦。余居石林，与云茅南北正相望，故四章皆及之云。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526725_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　是年，在建康府任，为方勺文集作跋。作品：《书方勺云茅漫录后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216750' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216750' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216750?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书方勺云茅漫录后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216750")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216750_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216750'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216750'>仁声，余少时识之埸屋中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216750_comment'></div>博学多闻，不专为举子文词，尤刻意作诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216750_comment'></div>客扬州，帅丞相苏公子容厚礼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216750_comment'></div>喜交当世名士，遇其所合，倾家赀具馔，歌呼饮酒穷日夜，士亦以此乐从之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216750_comment'></div>家坐是贫，仁声不悔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216750_comment'></div>既老，结庐吴兴西溪之上，因诵杜子美诗，至「何时一茅屋，送老白云边」，欣然以为与其意会，乃名其居曰「云茅庵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216750_comment'></div>平生诗文甚多，皆随手散去，不复录，独取近岁所存藁，次为《云茅漫录》十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216750_comment'></div>余镇建康，仁声年七十六矣，间关自吴兴特来见余，意气尚不衰，曰：「吾亦安用此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216750_comment'></div>尚使后来居是溪者知有吾姓名尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216750_comment'></div>兵兴以来，四方游旧零落殆尽，存者不过三四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216750_comment'></div>仁声又居同郡，时时数往来，其可无一言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216750_comment'></div>然仁声自言尝从方士得服气炼形法，其貌瘠而不枯，风月胜时，好事者能数载酒往过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216750_comment'></div>其为云茅之储，固未已也，乃书其后归之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1216750_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年10月</a>　在建康府任，十月七日前后，作《徽宗皇帝挽歌词五首》其一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《徽宗皇帝挽歌词五首》其二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《徽宗皇帝挽歌词五首》其三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《徽宗皇帝挽歌词五首》其四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《徽宗皇帝挽歌词五首》其五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526731' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526731' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526731?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽宗皇帝挽歌词五首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526731")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526731_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526731'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526731'>制作三王旧，忧勤一纪馀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526731'>岂惟成礼乐，真欲混车书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526731'>黼扆犹丹陛，飙轮忽紫虚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526731'>帝乡归路稳，无复顾楼居。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526731'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526731_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526732' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526732' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526732?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526732_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526732'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526732'>帝业承瓜瓞，天伦映棣华。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526732'>千年垂接统，四海自为家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526732'>毕郢终何恨，苍梧邈已赊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526732'>庙壖惊指顾，行路泣悲笳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526732'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526732_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526733' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526733' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526733?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526733_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526733'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526733'>脱屣初无恋，遗弓故不忘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526733'>金盘徒自耸，玉碗且深藏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526733'>付托归真主，经营有旧章。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526733'>柏城森渭水，空愧寝中郎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526733'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526733_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526734' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526734' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526734?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526734_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526734'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526734'>卜宅轩台近，因山禹穴深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526734'>缀衣惊在匣，黄屋本非<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作无）</span>心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526734'>海阔青云隔，天高白日沉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526734'>秋风无马迹，惆怅属车音。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526734'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526734_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526735' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526735' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526735?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526735_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526735'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526735'>浴殿陪书诏，甘泉忝侍臣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526735'>虚传游帝所，不复从时巡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526735'>效死终何日，馀生漫此身。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526735'>攀髯如<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作知）</span>已矣，挥涕洒江滨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526735'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526735_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年10月</a>　在建康府任，十月七日前后，作《徽宗皇帝祭文三首》其一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《徽宗皇帝祭文三首》其二《留守司》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《徽宗皇帝祭文三首》之《建康府》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216782' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216782' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216782?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽宗皇帝祭文<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　安抚司）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216782")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216782_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216782'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216782'>天步初艰，为中原而远狩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216782_comment'></div>帝乡不返，倾率土以缠哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216782_comment'></div>逖闻灵御之怀，弥切遗弓之慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216782_comment'></div>威容如在，伟烈具存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216782_comment'></div>参帝王步骤之馀，皆期力致；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216782_comment'></div>接天地混茫之化，独以心成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216782_comment'></div>俄兴无妄之灾，莫测盖高之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216782_comment'></div>虽神游八极，固无尔界之殊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216782_comment'></div>而梦锡九龄，终屈群生之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216782_comment'></div>臣顷持从橐，尝迩垂旒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216782_comment'></div>永怀未报之恩，攀髯已远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216782_comment'></div>徒抱无穷之恋，陨涕何追！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216782_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1216782_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽宗皇帝祭文<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　留守司）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216783")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216783_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216783'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216783'>应期抚运，悼历数之有终；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216783_comment'></div>绍业承休，仰威灵之如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216783_comment'></div>神游不远，仗卫来还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216783_comment'></div>爰追在宥之初，实际承平之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216783_comment'></div>典章文物，粲方册以具存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216783_comment'></div>华夏蛮夷，奠海隅而咸服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216783_comment'></div>岂期祸变，横起遐陬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216783_comment'></div>抚恒岳以北巡，既穷朔易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216783_comment'></div>越函关而西度，宁间流沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216783_comment'></div>俄成脱屣之游，莫极垂衣之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216783_comment'></div>臣拘縻郡绂，阻造灵輴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216783_comment'></div>泣血书辞，固难名于大造；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216783_comment'></div>铭心戴德，徒自结于孤忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216783_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1216783_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216784' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216784' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216784?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽宗皇帝祭文<span class='inlineComment2'>（三　建康府）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216784")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216784_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216784'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216784'>神凝帝所，孰测真游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216784_comment'></div>泽在人心，难忘孺慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216784_comment'></div>望銮舆之来复，追玉几之始冯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216784_comment'></div>力图斯民，宁惮戎车之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216784_comment'></div>归格艺祖，莫闻清跸之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216784_comment'></div>痛裂五情，哀缠九土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216784_comment'></div>载念忧勤之迹，尤高继述之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216784_comment'></div>周历更传，方赖延洪之绪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216784_comment'></div>尧仁广被，尚怀遏密之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216784_comment'></div>臣拘守封圻，阻趋仗卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216784_comment'></div>揽涕苍梧之野，陈迹空存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216784_comment'></div>驰心汾水之阳，馀生永已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216784_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1216784_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年12月12日</a>　在建康，十月十二日，移帅福州。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
寿县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='820a09e7f2fc45099402f89ef7b9ccdb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("820a09e7f2fc45099402f89ef7b9ccdb");'><span id='820a09e7f2fc45099402f89ef7b9ccdb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>，64岁</div><div id='820a09e7f2fc45099402f89ef7b9ccdb' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>六月初，视师至寿春。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>六月十一日前，在寿春八公山下，有再遣晁公昂觇师诗。作品：《闻兀术将过淮再遣晁公昂觇师》<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作《闻敌兵将过淮再遣晁公昂觇师》许文可。）</span><div id='poem_526662' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526662' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526662?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻兀朮将过淮再遣晁公昂觇师</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_526662")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_526662_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526662'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526662'>狂酋屡惯骋长驱，未省新军有被庐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526662'>快饮勿辞金凿落，先声须破铁浮图<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526662'>䞤官尔自疲千里<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，飞将吾宁较一夫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526662'>试向八公山上望，当关何用守濡须<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526662'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526662'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_526662_0'>⑴ 自注：时张、韩两军（影宋本作帅）治师甚肃，士极贾勇。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_526662_0'>⑵ 自注：鞍虏将下亲兵皆精练，号铁浮图。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_526662_0'>⑶ 自注：虏遣师往来国中，号䞤官，日行数百里。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_526662_0'>⑷ 自注：寿阳为江淮襟喉，曹操先得之，故军每至濡须。东晋能保有，故谢玄有淝水之捷云。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526662_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>六月十一日前，在寿春八公山，有词。作品：《八声甘州·寿阳楼八公山作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_80250' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_80250' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/80250?labeling=true' target='_blank'>八声甘州<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>寿阳楼八公山作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_80250")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_80250_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_80250'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_80250'>故都迷岸草，望长淮、依然绕孤城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_80250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_80250'>想乌衣年少，芝兰秀发，戈戟云横。<div id='poem_sentence_1_80250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_80250'>坐看骄兵南渡，沸浪骇奔鲸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_80250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_80250'>转眄东流水，一顾功成。<div id='poem_sentence_3_80250_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_80250'>千载八公山下，尚断崖草木，遥拥峥嵘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_80250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_80250'>漫云涛吞吐，无处问豪英。<div id='poem_sentence_5_80250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_80250'>信劳生、空成今古，笑我来、何事怆遗情。<div id='poem_sentence_6_80250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_80250'>东山老，可堪岁晚，独听桓筝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_80250_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_80250'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(80250)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
滁州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1b14b003c04e43edad8e17d9a94d3eb1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1b14b003c04e43edad8e17d9a94d3eb1");'><span id='1b14b003c04e43edad8e17d9a94d3eb1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>，64岁</div><div id='1b14b003c04e43edad8e17d9a94d3eb1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　秋，在濠州，有《水调歌头》词。作品：《水调歌头·濠州观鱼台作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_80263' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_80263' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/80263?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>濠州观鱼台作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_80263")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_80263_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_80263'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_80263'>渺渺楚天阔，秋水去无穷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_80263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_80263'>两淮不辨牛马，轻浪舞回风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_80263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_80263'>独倚高台一笑，圉圉游鱼来往，还戏此波中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_80263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_80263'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_80263", 80263, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>危槛</span>对千里，落日照澄空。<div id='poem_sentence_3_80263_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_80263'>子非我，安知我，意真同。<div id='poem_sentence_4_80263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_80263'>鹏飞鹍化何有，沧海漫冲融。<div id='poem_sentence_5_80263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_80263'>堪笑磻溪遗老，白首直钩溪畔，岁晚忽衰翁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_80263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_80263'>功业竟安在，徒自兆非熊。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_80263_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
福建
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3eb67ba94f7a48ab96fc64ef83b2ef19_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3eb67ba94f7a48ab96fc64ef83b2ef19");'><span id='3eb67ba94f7a48ab96fc64ef83b2ef19_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>，67岁</div><div id='3eb67ba94f7a48ab96fc64ef83b2ef19' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年2月6日</a>　二月六日，入福建界。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f06c42543bab40abbe01cbcded3f763e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f06c42543bab40abbe01cbcded3f763e");'><span id='f06c42543bab40abbe01cbcded3f763e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>，67岁</div><div id='f06c42543bab40abbe01cbcded3f763e' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>二月，在福建路，有奏札。作品：《奏乞遇本路讨贼权令江西广东官吏听节制札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span>《奏见留南剑州措置讨荡刘大小老状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216642?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞遇本路讨贼权令江西广东官吏听节制劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216642")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216642'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216642'>臣今月初二日将带高举官兵行至信州铅山县界，据福建路转运司并南剑州状申：本路见有杨头陀、刘和、刘小老等贼火不一，于南剑、汀、漳州尤溪、沙县、清流、宁化、莲城、漳岩等三州六县出没作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216642_comment'></div>正月二十五日，又有南剑州将乐县赖保一头项，宰杀祭神，杀人放火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216642_comment'></div>乞催高举军前来应援捉杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216642_comment'></div>臣已即时遣发高举选精锐一千五百人，星夜蹉程径赴南剑州，臣亦一面相继前去措画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216642_comment'></div>已具奏闻外，契勘福建盗贼，自来系与江西虔、吉、广东循、梅两路更为表里，每乘州县间隙，即啸聚窃发，若遇官军讨荡，即便分散，各于邻近路分逃避，以此逗遛日月，无缘成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216642_comment'></div>臣今来既行措置讨捕，窃虑贼徒惧见官军声势，不敢迎敌，依前于两路州县走透，难以追逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216642_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降睿旨，疾速行下江西、广东帅司及提刑司，各于贼徒自来经涉往还要害去处分布军兵，预行把截等待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216642_comment'></div>如遇本路进兵讨捕之时，其两路官吏并权暂听臣节制，约日并举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216642_comment'></div>庶几首尾相应，事体齐一，各肯公共协心，贼势穷蹙，日近可以破灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216642_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216642_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1216642_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1216643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216643?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏见留南剑州措置讨荡刘大小老状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216643")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216643'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216643'>右，臣恭被圣训，将带高举官兵二千人前来本路措置盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216643_comment'></div>正月十七日行至宣州宁国县界，准枢密院劄子，备据泉州奏，漳州龙岩县有贼马侵入泉州永春县市，令臣疾速措置施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216643_comment'></div>续又准枢密院劄子，备坐本路转运司、南剑州申，永春县贼作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216643_comment'></div>并据转运司、南剑州申，漳、汀、南剑州管界见有杨头陀、刘和、刘小老、赖保等贼徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216643_comment'></div>臣即时先遣高举兵二千五百人星夜径往南剑州，臣亦相继起发，不住节次行下本路州县将佐，多方防托讨捕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216643_comment'></div>今月初六日，入本路界交割安抚使职事，各具状奏闻外，臣十二日已到南剑州，体问得贼徒除杨头陀、刘和一火已经广东副总管韩京及统领官曹韶杀散，陈八癞一火被本路人兵杀逐出江西界，吴二十五一火被江西人马捕获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216643_comment'></div>馀外止有刘大小老一火在南剑州接漳、泉州界往来出没，冲溃官军，及赖保一火乞就招安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216643_comment'></div>臣见留南剑州分布高举并本司先差到焦缜等官兵，及属县巡尉下弓手土兵等，于刘大小老啸聚去处，四面把截去处，量度事势，会合兵民尅日并力讨荡，并审实赖保情伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216643_comment'></div>候见次第，别具奏闻次，谨录奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216643_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1216643_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>二月，在福建路，用三策弥盗，颇为监司所议。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e1db4f1f9b374b1989b0a8fe7930960e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e1db4f1f9b374b1989b0a8fe7930960e");'><span id='e1db4f1f9b374b1989b0a8fe7930960e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>，69岁</div><div id='e1db4f1f9b374b1989b0a8fe7930960e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　春，自福州回卞山山居。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
福州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8a9afe66cd85442d9413cad4ab24d746_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8a9afe66cd85442d9413cad4ab24d746");'><span id='8a9afe66cd85442d9413cad4ab24d746_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1144')">1143-1144年</a>，67-68岁</div><div id='8a9afe66cd85442d9413cad4ab24d746' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年3月</a>　在知福州任，三月，有奏札。作品：《奏本路讨补盗贼略尽乞下江西广东帅司提刑司乘时措置札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216644?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏本路讨捕盗贼略尽乞下江西广东帅司提刑司乘时措置劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216644")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216644'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216644'>臣恭被圣训，将带高举官兵前来措置本路盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216644_comment'></div>续准尚书省劄子，备坐本路转运司等奏贼人赖保等作过，奉圣旨催臣疾速措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216644_comment'></div>寻发遣高举兵径赴南剑州，臣亦追逐起发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216644_comment'></div>至二月初六日入本路界，交割安抚司职事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216644_comment'></div>十二日到南剑州，躬亲询究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216644_comment'></div>贼党自去冬以来，共有杨头陀等五六火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216644_comment'></div>除杨头陀、刘和二火已为知循州韩京杀散，陈八癞一火为本路兵逐出江西界，并吴二十五一火为江西捕获，目今止有刘大小老、赖保两火见在南剑州界内屯聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216644_comment'></div>臣先已节次行下本路将佐焦缜等分路防守把截，贼不得动，势已穷蹙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216644_comment'></div>见增添高举兵前去会审度贼势，相共随机进讨，日近可以败获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216644_comment'></div>缘刘大小老本是虔贼，侵入本界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216644_comment'></div>访闻江西、广东目今皆有贼盗未获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216644_comment'></div>今来臣本道虽能讨捕略尽，若两路不一并除灭，即不免却有伺间入本路界，无由可绝后患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216644_comment'></div>体问得知循州韩京、江西路分钤辖程师回各有材武，深知捕贼利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216644_comment'></div>止缘从前隔路不相照应，遂致奸猾之党互为出入，轻侮官司，迁延岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216644_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降睿旨下两路帅臣并提刑司，乘时协力措置，仍专委韩京、程师回捉杀，庶几三路并得平定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216644_comment'></div>所有以后合行经久利便，臣见广行询访，各尽土俗所宜，类聚条画，别具奏陈次，谨具劄子冒闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216644_comment'></div>干渎天威，臣无任惶惧激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216644_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1216644_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年6月1日</a>　六月初一，在福州，与张元干游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年6月1日</a>　六月初一，在福州，跋张元干《幽岩尊祖事实》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年6月23日</a>　在知福州任，六月二十三日，有奏议。作品：《奏措置分捕过盗贼火数官兵各已回军状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216648?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏措置分捕过盗贼火数官兵各已回军状<span class='inlineComment2'>（亥六月二十三日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年6月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216648")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216648_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216648'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216648'>右，臣昨奉圣旨，将带高举军二千人前来本路措置盗贼，节次承准枢密院劄子，备坐本路转运、提刑司、南剑州申，汀、漳、南剑州管界有杨头陀、刘和、刘小老、赖保等作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216648_comment'></div>二月初六日，臣入本路界后，续据漳、汀、泉、南剑州诸处申，管下又有陈八癞、吴二十五、刘大老、陈勇、赖权、曾志、凌铁弹、吴和尚等贼徒出没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216648_comment'></div>臣寻遣发高举与本路将分布地分讨捕，并移文广东副总管韩京、江西钤辖程师回等前来会合，并力追袭，及提点刑狱公事方庭实躬亲前来监督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216648_comment'></div>除高举先杀散陈勇、赖权，即是刘大小老其人昨已被官兵杀死，系陈勇等假托逐人姓名外，杨头陀、刘和一火先被韩京、曹韶杀散招捉了当，赖保一火招谕归业，陈八癞一火系本路人兵散逐出江西界，被程师回等生擒，吴二十五一火亦被程师回擒获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216648_comment'></div>所有陈勇继被高举、韩京军杀降，已解赴枢密院，赖权杀散遁走出潮州界，曾志一火被韩京擒获，凌铁弹一火被将官翟皋、卢真杀散，吴和尚一火被清流县尉擒获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216648_comment'></div>唯漳州界内何一、李官等残党三两火各不及一二百人，皆藏匿山林险阻之地，兵将不可深入，难以久驻伺候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216648_comment'></div>除已行下本处巡尉官兵探伺贼党出没，乘便掩捕，务要日近净尽，至五月终，汀、泉、南剑州管下已前贼火并已杀捕了当，别无未获人数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216648_comment'></div>所有先遣发诸头项兵将，各已勾回驻劄去处；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216648_comment'></div>其汀、泉、南剑、漳州界上把截防守官兵乡兵，亦已放散；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216648_comment'></div>韩京、程师回已回广东、江西；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216648_comment'></div>提刑方庭实已归本司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216648_comment'></div>并高举回军，于六月初二日到福州讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216648_comment'></div>谨录奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216648_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1216648_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年7月8日</a>　在知福州任，七月八日，有奏状。作品：《奏乞将残破州县今年税赋量行蠲减状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216649?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞将残破州县今年税赋量行蠲减状<span class='inlineComment2'>（亥七月八日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年7月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216649")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216649'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216649'>右，臣契勘本路自去年以来，相继有盗贼吴阙四等二十馀火，侵犯汀、漳、泉、剑四州一十三县管下，往来焚劫，杀人作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216649_comment'></div>民被驱虏，或遭杀戮，或有逃散，缘此田地抛荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216649_comment'></div>兼以会合诸头项大军防守讨捕，所用钱粮万数浩瀚，州县应办不前，不无科借于民，内汀、漳二州尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216649_comment'></div>日近并已讨捕破灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216649_comment'></div>节次据广东总管韩京、统制高举并本司属官彭世范申，提领军马自入汀州上杭县界，田地抛荒，不住据税户陈乞蠲减税赋等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216649_comment'></div>检会绍兴元年三月内□贼范汝为作过之后，本路安抚使程迈被奉下诏，条具便民利物事，内一项，残破州县人民乞量行放免税租。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216649_comment'></div>奉圣旨，令转运、提刑司体究，委经残破州县，与将今年夏秋二税减免三分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216649_comment'></div>又绍兴十一年七月内，权知汀州张宪代劄子，为上杭、武平两县累因兵火，民力凋瘵，乞权免上供钱物、军器、物料等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216649_comment'></div>奉圣旨，武平、上杭两县合起上供钱银特与免二年，其上供军器、物料等令转运司相度减免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216649_comment'></div>今来汀、漳等州管下委是去年以来累经盗贼焚劫，频经科借，人户重困，深可矜悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216649_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降睿旨下转运、提刑司，于逐州屯驻人兵县分，实经残破、乡民失业去处，许依前例，将合输纳今年夏秋二税并上供钱银、军器、物料等，特与量行蠲减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216649_comment'></div>庶使幽远凋瘵之民，得沾朝廷实惠，免致失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216649_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1216649_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年8月15日</a>　八月中秋在闽中宴客，张元干、富直柔等与焉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年8月15日</a>　八月中秋在闽中宴客，赋《念奴娇》作品：《念奴娇·中秋宴客有怀壬午岁吴江长桥》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_80279' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_80279' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/80279?labeling=true' target='_blank'>念奴娇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>中秋宴客，有怀壬午岁吴江长桥</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_80279")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_80279_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_80279'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_80279'>洞庭波冷，望冰轮初转，沧海沈沈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_80279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_80279'>万顷孤光云阵卷，长笛吹破层阴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_80279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_80279'>汹涌三江，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_80279", 80279, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>银涛</span>无际，遥带五湖深。<div id='poem_sentence_2_80279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_80279'>酒阑歌罢，至今鼍怒龙吟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_80279_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_80279'>回首江海平生，漂流容易散，佳期难寻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_80279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_80279'>缥缈高城风露爽，独倚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_80279", 80279, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>危槛</span>重临。<div id='poem_sentence_5_80279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_80279'>醉倒清尊，姮娥应笑，犹有向来心。<div id='poem_sentence_6_80279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
