ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年8月15日</a>　八月中秋在闽中宴客，赋《念奴娇》，张元干代富直柔答之，即席作《念奴娇·代洛滨次石林韵》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年8月26日</a>　在知福州任，八月二十六日，有奏状。作品：《奏福兴巡检仍兼统领水军就辟乔昌祖状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216650?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏福兴巡检仍兼统领水军就辟乔昌祖状<span class='inlineComment2'>（亥八月二十六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年8月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216650")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216650'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216650'>检准枢密院绍兴九年四月十二日劄子：「枢密院奏，吏部申：『福建路安抚使司申请措置海道事件，内一项，相度将福兴都巡检寨移于连江县管下荻芦门置立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216650_comment'></div>今契勘福兴都巡检下招募水军，已见就绪，欲将福兴都巡检使，以安抚使司水军统领兼福州兴化军都巡检使为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216650_comment'></div>奉圣旨依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216650_comment'></div>本部勘会，依条合差注巡检窠阙虽元系本选，认定合差注在部大使臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216650_comment'></div>今来福建安抚司申，将本部见使福州兴化军都巡检使阙以安抚使司水军统领兼福州兴化军都巡检使为名，本部即未审上件窠阙系今后许□□□差注在部大使臣，唯复是合从朝廷一面使阙差人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216650_comment'></div>致本部未敢直便施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216650_comment'></div>若许将上件阙从本部依旧使阙，缘本部别无差注统领官条法，只乞以福州兴化军都巡检使兼安抚使司水军统领为名，更合取自朝廷指挥』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216650_comment'></div>右，奉圣旨，将上件阙权令本路帅司奏辟合入资序大使臣，候事宁息日，依旧劄付本司照会施行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216650_comment'></div>右，契勘本司昨依前项指挥，奏辟武翼郎张山，已成资满罢讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216650_comment'></div>今来见任人敦武郎陈舆系准尚书省劄差到，于今年七月二十一日到任，即未有替人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216650_comment'></div>缘本路抵接广东、两浙，海洋阔远，时被逐处贼船出没侵扰，全藉谙晓海道统领官弹压，水军往来巡捕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216650_comment'></div>合依前项指挥辟官替陈舆成资阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216650_comment'></div>本司今窃见忠训郎、閤门祗候乔昌祖委有才武，谙识海道，堪充上件差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216650_comment'></div>已取到乔昌祖愿就及无应合回避亲戚文状，并录白出身以来文字与脚色、家状、印纸，委福州通判、左朝奉大夫程滂等点对审量覆实，委无差漏，保明诣实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216650_comment'></div>其录白文字连粘在前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216650_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降睿旨，差忠训郎、閤门祗候乔昌祖充安抚使司水军统领兼福州兴化军都巡检使，替敦武郎陈舆成资满阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216650_comment'></div>所贵海道得人，缓急可以倚仗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216650_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1216650_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年10月16日</a>　在知福州任，十月十六日，有奏状。作品：《申尚书省拟定五县赏格状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216689' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216689' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216689?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申尚书省拟定五县赏格状<span class='inlineComment2'>（亥十月六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年10月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216689")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216689_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216689'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216689'>右，契勘本路自来盗贼窃发，多在汀、漳，次则南剑、泉四州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216689_comment'></div>汀州上杭、武平、莲城，漳州龙岩、漳浦五县，并与江西、广东虔、循、□□□□皆是险阻瘴恶之地，其民凭恃险阻，内外连结，更相往来，无岁不啸聚作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216689_comment'></div>其次汀州宁化、清流、长汀、漳州龙溪、泉州永春、安溪、德化、南剑州尤溪、沙县九县，亦皆地分比近，贼徒乘间冲突出没之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216689_comment'></div>各去本州三五程，帅司十程以上，缓急难以救应，以此奸猾无所畏惮，公肆猖蹶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216689_comment'></div>惟藉知县、巡尉得人，究心职事，平时备御有方，缓急随宜措画，乃可防弭后患，不失机会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216689_comment'></div>窃缘其地多是水土恶弱，官吏不肯注授，纵有到任，寻亦托故要去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216689_comment'></div>若非增立赏典，重行劝诱，终难责办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216689_comment'></div>伏见祖宗旧制，南恩州阳春县令任满，与改合入官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216689_comment'></div>漳州龙岩、漳浦、汀州上杭、武平、莲城五县任满，有改官举主二员，与改合入官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1216689_comment'></div>无举主，循一资，占射差遣一次；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1216689_comment'></div>簿尉不该改官人循一资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1216689_comment'></div>今来龙岩、漳浦、上杭、武平、莲城五县亦系素多瘴疠，盗贼巢穴，与阳春县事体略同，欲望朝廷详酌，特命有司参定先次将前件县分并别立选格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1216689_comment'></div>知县注曾更历民事、无私罪人，每月更给茶汤钱，仍递增赏典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1216689_comment'></div>内龙岩、漳浦、上杭、武平、莲城五县任满无私罪，与依阳春县例，县令改合入官，其京朝官与转一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1216689_comment'></div>宁化、清流、长汀、龙溪四县，令却依龙岩旧法，有改官举主二员或三员，与改官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1216689_comment'></div>永春、安溪、德化、尤溪、沙县五县，即县令人与循一资，占射差遣，改官人减二年磨勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1216689_comment'></div>巡尉依逐县知□比类降等施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1216689_comment'></div>庶几人知激励，皆肯乐从，本司亦可督责委办职事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1216689_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省，伏候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1216689_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　是年，当在福州，张元干有《叶少蕴生朝》诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　在知福州任，春日，与李弥逊同游鼓山，有诗唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年5月16日</a>　在知福州任，五月十六日，有奏状。作品：《申枢密院乞将明溪为镇置监镇巡检状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216692' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216692' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216692?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申枢密院乞将明溪为镇置监镇巡检状<span class='inlineComment2'>（子五月十六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年5月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216692")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216692_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216692'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216692'>契勘明溪南至沙县，北至宁化，西至清流，东至将乐县，系在四县之中，相去皆不啻二百里以上，周环几千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216692_comment'></div>去官司远，寻常官吏法令不及，以此风俗习为强犷，赋税多不输纳，无所忌惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216692_comment'></div>日前本路兵官王进领兵经由，至烧断桥，不肯放过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216692_comment'></div>去年本司差属官会合高举，人亦聚众惊恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216692_comment'></div>若不因此措置，终为后患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216692_comment'></div>今博采人言，皆欲将明溪立为烟火镇，差监镇一员，置巡检一员，召募土兵三百人，以时弹压巡捕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216692_comment'></div>虽不免岁有小费，然与其啸聚窃发，害及良民，兴起官兵，用度不赀，犹为利便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216692_comment'></div>近据马钦军前亦具到上件利害，伏望朝廷特赐详察施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1216692_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年5月19日</a>　在知福州任，五月十九日，有奏状。作品：《申枢密院乞改明溪巡检为清流等三县巡检状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216693' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216693' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216693?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申枢密院乞改明溪巡检为清流等三县巡检状<span class='inlineComment2'>（子五月十九日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年5月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216693")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216693_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216693'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216693'>近具申明，欲于日近汀州清流县明溪俞彻明作过地分创立为镇，增置巡检一员，召募土兵三百人，弹压一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216693_comment'></div>已奉圣旨依所乞，令某疾速施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216693_comment'></div>除已一面措置外，契勘明溪地里，东至将乐一百二十里，西至清流一百一十五里，南至沙县一百八十里，北至宁化一百四十里，最为阔远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216693_comment'></div>内地名檀石，去明溪六十里，俗尤为犷悍，自来居民多不纳苗税，杀伤□□□□不能以法治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216693_comment'></div>今来巡检廨宇欲于檀石建立，以汀州清流、南剑州将乐、沙县三县巡检兼巡捉茶盐贼盗公事为名，先□踏逐，致杀获俞彻明，第二名□□□赖文盛初不曾从贼，颇有□□，仍有上件劳绩，本□□依□□续降到空名官告书填与承节郎讫，并具申明，乞就辟充巡检□□回降指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216693_comment'></div>今来盗贼平定之初，正□□察防闲，除已逐急差本人前去权摄处置一行事务□，委汀州依立限召募军兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216693_comment'></div>其监镇官许于本路寄居见任官内踏逐强干通知事宜者，同提刑司奏差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1216693_comment'></div>伏望特赐施行<span class='inlineComment2'>（《石林奏议》卷一五。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1216693_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1216693'>致：原缺，据右引补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1216693_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年9月8日</a>　在知福州任，九月八日，有奏状。作品：《申枢密院乞下浙西沿海县权暂禁止贩米以绝朱明粮食状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（许文可。）</span><div id='poem_1216694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1216694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1216694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申枢密院乞下浙西沿海州县权暂禁止贩米以绝朱明粮食状<span class='inlineComment2'>（子九月初八日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年9月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24994, "宋", "叶梦得", "poem_title_1216694")'>叶梦得</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1216694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1216694'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1216694'>契勘本司见讨捕海贼朱明，先须绝其粮道，使阙食坐困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1216694_comment'></div>虽不住行下沿海地分严设堤防，不得纵令上岸打虏米谷禾稻，缘沿海诸县自来系于两浙西路贩秀州华亭等处米斛为业，每船动是数百石或千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1216694_comment'></div>前月中旬间，朱明粮食已绝，访闻忽有自华亭贩米回来海洋，与朱明泊船处相近，忽被要截，即便以所载米献朱明为言，因免杀戮，仍给价直增倍，遂得再振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1216694_comment'></div>欲乞下浙西湖、秀州、平江府、江阴军等处境内滨海州县，权暂禁止，不许贩米前来福州，违者重坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1216694_comment'></div>候事平日，依旧不过一两月间，于商贾别无重害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1216694_comment'></div>欲望朝廷特赐指挥施行，□□具申尚书省，伏候指挥<span class='inlineComment2'>（《石林奏议》卷一五。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1216694_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1216694'>具：原缺，据汲古阁本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1216694_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　是年，在知福州任，石林故祖羲叟追封福国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　是年，在知福州任，石林故祖母刘氏赠韩国夫人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　是年，在知福州任，石林故父助赠太傅。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　是年，在知福州任，石林故母晁氏赠镇国夫人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　是年，在知福州任，韩元吉至福州拜访石林。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　是年，在府治建万象亭。富直柔有《题万象亭并序》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　是年，在府治建万象亭。韩元吉有《万象亭赋序》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年12月11日</a>　在福州，十二月十一日，由左大中大夫迁为左通议大夫，提举临安洞霄宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　在福州，年底，张元干有《叶少蕴生朝三首》贺石林生辰。<br /></div>
